BFS 工廠常使用大型儲料筒倉（Silos）存放大量樹脂。這些設備的風險點：

  • 水分累積：塑膠樹脂吸濕後可能影響成型品質，還可能促進微生物生長。
  • 清潔挑戰：大型筒倉難以定期清潔，需要建立定期清空-清洗-消毒的 SOP。
  • 監測策略：定期取樣監測倉內樹脂的微生物負荷和濕度。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為何 BFS 製程中需要監測樹脂的內毒素（Endotoxin）？擠出過程的高溫是否足以消除內毒素風險？
  2. BFS 工廠的換型（Resin Changeover）需要哪些特別程序？為何需要確保輸送管線和擠出機的清除（Clearance）？
Topic K.3: Blow-Fill-Seal Process Simulation (p31–p32)

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement

What are the unique APS considerations for the BFS process?

Recommendation

APS for BFS should be conducted in the same manner as non-BFS aseptic processes.

Rationale

The level of automation, absence of inherent interventions, and visibility of media contamination in translucent, pigmented, or opaque plastic containers should be taken into consideration when designing the APS, as they would be in any aseptic filling process.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — BFS APS 的特殊考量

雖然 PDA PtC-1 說 BFS 的 APS 應「以相同方式進行」，但在實際執行時有幾個重要的特殊考量：

  • 高度自動化（High Automation）：BFS 通常沒有人員直接在充填區操作，因此 APS 中「干預模擬」的設計需要特別思考——哪些是 BFS 固有的干預？（如機器停機、Parison 問題處理等）
  • 容器不透明/半透明問題：BFS 常用半透明或著色塑膠容器。培養基（通常是 TSB，黃褐色）在這類容器中，污染生長產生的渾濁可能不易目視判別，需要特殊的判讀 SOP 或輔助檢測方法。
  • APS 頻率：PDA TR22 規定每半年至少一次，BFS 通常不需更頻繁——但因其高自動化程度，一旦有 APS 失敗，追查原因往往更困難。

重點提示 — 培養基可見度問題的監管關注

FDA 查核時曾對 BFS 的 APS 結果判讀提出疑問：「你如何確認半透明容器內沒有微生物生長？」

建議的實務做法：

  • 使用透明版本的相同塑膠配方（如果可行）進行 APS，以提高可見度。
  • 如果使用一般生產材料，建立額外的培養基目視判讀 SOP（例如背光照射、傾斜觀察）。
  • 在 APS 計畫中明確說明「可見度限制」及補償措施，並獲得 QA 批准。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個 BFS APS 使用的是著色（藍色）塑膠容器。培養基為 TSB（澄清黃棕色）。你如何設計 APS 的污染判讀方法？需要哪些額外的 SOP？
  2. BFS 高度自動化，幾乎不需要人員干預——那麼 BFS 的 APS 需要模擬哪些「干預」？（提示：考慮機器異常、物料補充等場景。）
Topic L: Air Locks (p32–p34)

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement

Are separate air locks required for materials and for personnel to move into critical zones in order to prevent contamination?

Recommendation

Where possible, sterilized materials should be directly transferred into the critical zones after sterilization through double-door sterilizers or decontamination through other aseptic transfer devices. Where this is not performed, or cannot be performed, entry to these areas should be through separate air locks with an active air supply for (1) personnel and (2) equipment and materials.

Where it is not possible or feasible to physically separate the movement of personnel and materials or to have separate air locks, time-based separation of movement by procedure should be considered. Where an assessment aligned with the CCS indicates that the risk of contamination is high, however, separate rooms for personnel and material entering and leaving production areas should be used.

The final area of a gowning room should be in at-rest (as-built) conditions of the same grade as the area into which this area leads. The entrance into and exit from critical zones and Grade A and Grade B, including gowning rooms, should be through separate air locks or entrances.

Gowning rooms for entrances into and exits from the controlled and graded areas should be designed with air locks and used to provide physical separation of the different stages of gowning and, thus, minimize microbial and particulate contamination of protective clothing and more highly controlled areas.

For equipment and materials, separate air locks for entrances and exits should be considered. If separate air locks are not possible, procedures should be in place to prevent entrances and exits without intermediate cleaning or sanitization.

Rationale

The control of contamination as a result of personnel and material movement can be achieved through the segregation of entities, by means of the:

  • Design of the process (e.g., double-door sterilizers)
  • Use of separate air locks for personnel and materials
  • Unidirectional flow of personnel and materials
  • Use of active air supply in the air locks
  • Use of interlocks and timed procedures for the opening of sequential airlock entrances

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 氣閘（Air Lock）的設計原則

氣閘（Air Lock）是不同等級潔淨區域之間的過渡緩衝空間，功能類似於隔離不同壓力環境的「緩衝區」。其設計應符合以下原則：

  • 人員與物料分開：人員更衣氣閘和物料傳遞氣閘應分開設置，避免交叉污染。
  • 最終更衣室等級匹配：最終更衣區（脫下外衣、穿好潔淨服的最後一步）必須達到與其通往區域相同等級的靜止條件。
  • 主動供氣：氣閘應有自己的獨立送風系統（Active Air Supply），而不僅僅依賴相鄰房間的空氣滲入。
  • 互鎖（Interlock）：防止兩側門同時開啟，確保任何時刻只有一扇門是開著的。

比喻說明 — 氣閘像水壩的閘門系統

想像一個運河閘門系統（船閘）：高水位區（Grade A 或 B）和低水位區（Grade C 或 D）之間，透過一個可控制的「閘門空間」連接。進入時先進入閘門空間，關閉後方門，改變水位（等效：關閉氣閘、恢復壓力差），然後才能開啟前方門。

潔淨室氣閘的「水位」對應「壓力差」：

  • Grade A/B 通常是正壓（避免外部空氣流入）
  • 氣閘是「過渡壓力」的緩衝區
  • 互鎖確保兩側不會同時開啟，防止「水（空氣）溢出」

PDA PtC-1 還提到一個更簡單的解決方案：雙門滅菌器（Double-Door Sterilizer）——就像水壩裡裝了一個「物料傳送管道」，物料直接從非潔淨側進入滅菌機，從潔淨側出來，完全不需要氣閘。

重點提示 — Grade B 更衣室的最終區域要求

PtC-1 明確規定：「更衣室的最終區域（final area）應在與其通往區域相同等級的靜止條件下運行。」

實務含義：如果更衣室通往 Grade B 充填室，那麼最終更衣區（穿上最後一層潔淨衣的地方）必須在靜止狀態下達到 Grade B 的粒子標準（ISO 5 等效）。這不僅是設計要求，也是更衣室的資格確認內容。

常見問題：許多老廠的更衣室「最終更衣區」沒有達到這個標準，或者沒有做過粒子計數確認——這是 EU Annex 1（2022）查核時的高頻缺陷點。

壓力梯度設計原則

典型壓力梯度設計（正壓保護模式）：

Grade A/B（充填室）    > Grade B（更衣/氣閘）   > Grade C（外走廊）

壓差建議值（依 EU Annex 1）：
相鄰區域之間：≥ 10–15 Pa

設計要點：
1. 氣閘應有獨立送風（不能只靠相鄰房間洩壓）
2. 互鎖系統：A 門開著時 B 門不能開
3. 單向人流和物流（進入/退出路線不交叉）
4. 緊急情況（如毒性或 OEB 高毒性產品）：
   使用「負壓氣閘」保護外部環境，
   而非保護內部

Grade A 為正壓的核心邏輯：
外部空氣（Grade C/D）不應流入 Grade A/B，
因此 Grade A/B 的壓力必須高於外部。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果因廠房限制無法設置獨立的人員氣閘和物料氣閘，PDA PtC-1 建議的替代方案是什麼？這個替代方案需要滿足哪些條件？
  2. Grade B 充填室的最終更衣區，在靜止狀態下應達到哪個 ISO 等級？這個要求應如何透過資格確認活動來驗證？
  3. 一個設施進行高毒性（OEB 5）產品的無菌充填，氣閘的壓力設計應為正壓還是負壓？為什麼？（這個問題超出 PtC-1 範疇，但考驗整合理解。）
Topic M: "At-Rest" and "In-Operation" Status (p34–p35)

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement

Should we test or monitor cleanrooms for total particulates in "at-rest" conditions in addition to "in-operation" conditions?

Recommendation

For qualification and regular requalification, both at-rest as well as in-operation test conditions should be used. Routine monitoring of at-rest conditions is not required as long as operational (total particulate) monitoring is in place.

Consideration should be given to the analysis of total particulate monitoring of base levels for processes that inherently generate process-related particles, for example, containers closed by fusion or processes that otherwise generate product-related particles. These may include processes related to BFS, form-fill-seal, and powder filling.

Rationale

At-rest conditions are reflective of design and initial operation and should be periodically verified (i.e., during requalification) to ensure that no significant changes have occurred.

At-rest monitoring may also be useful to establish baseline conditions that can be taken into consideration when setting in-process limits.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — At-Rest vs In-Operation 的定義

這是 EU Annex 1 和 ISO 14644 中非常基礎但容易混淆的概念：

  • At-Rest（靜止狀態）：潔淨室安裝完成、HVAC 運行，但無設備運轉、無人員在場。測試的是「環境本身」的潔淨能力。也稱為「As-Built」（剛建成）或「Unoccupied」（無人狀態）。
  • In-Operation（操作狀態）：生產設備正在運行，人員正在進行正常操作。測試的是「真實生產條件下」的潔淨室表現。

兩種狀態通常會有粒子數量差異（操作狀態通常粒子數更高），EU Annex 1 對 Grade A-D 都規定了兩種狀態的限值。

比喻說明 — At-Rest 是「空教室」，In-Operation 是「上課中」

想像一間學校教室：

  • At-Rest = 下課後清掃完畢的空教室：地板乾淨、空氣清新。這反映了「教室本身的清潔能力」。
  • In-Operation = 上課中（50 個學生坐在裡面）：粉筆灰、說話噴的飛沫、走動揚起的塵埃。這是「實際使用條件」。

資格確認時，兩種狀態都要測——你需要知道教室本身能達到多乾淨（At-Rest），也需要知道使用中還能維持什麼程度的潔淨（In-Operation）。但日常監測只要有「上課中」的監測就夠了——因為「上課中」的數據已經包含了最壞情況。

重點提示 — EU Annex 1 兩種狀態的粒子限值

等級 At-Rest ≥0.5µm (per m³) In-Operation ≥0.5µm (per m³)
Grade A 3,520 3,520
Grade B 3,520 352,000
Grade C 352,000 3,520,000
Grade D 3,520,000 未規定

注意 Grade A：At-Rest 和 In-Operation 的限值相同（3,520 per m³）。這表示 Grade A（通常是層流保護或 Isolator 內部）在操作過程中不應因人員活動而升高粒子數——這也是為什麼 Isolator/RABS 如此重要：它防止了人員成為 Grade A 區的粒子來源。

重點提示 — 製程產生粒子的特殊處理

PDA PtC-1 特別提到 BFS、Form-Fill-Seal（形成-充填-密封）和粉末充填等製程會本身產生粒子（製程相關粒子），不是環境污染的結果。

對這類製程，建議：

  • 先建立「沒有製程干擾時的基準（Baseline）」粒子水準
  • 用「相對偏差」（相對於基準的異常升高）來設定警戒和行動限值
  • 而非直接套用 ISO/EU 的絕對粒子數限值

這是 PDA 對監管框架的務實補充：標準數字是給一般情況用的，特殊製程需要特殊評估。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. PDA PtC-1 說日常監測不需要做 At-Rest 粒子監測——那麼什麼情況下需要重新做 At-Rest 測試？（提示：想想「定期重新確認（Requalification）」的觸發條件。）
  2. 一個粉末充填室（Grade B）的操作狀態粒子計數持續偏高，但 At-Rest 時完全符合標準。這意味著什麼？應如何調查？
Topic N: Sample Volume for Classification (p35–p36)

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement

What is the air volume, in relation to particles, to be sampled for classification purposes of cleanrooms?

Recommendation

The sample size described in the most current version of ISO 14644-1 should be used because this represents the current industry standard that is required by many regulators around the world.

Rationale

The ISO standard is based on scientific principles and industry expertise.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — ISO 14644-1 採樣量的計算

ISO 14644-1:2015 定義了每個採樣點的最小採樣量（Vs）：

計算公式：Vs = (20 / Cn,m) × 1000 (公升)

其中 Cn,m 是該潔淨等級在指定粒徑下的最大允許粒子濃度（per m³）。分子「20」代表統計學上需要捕獲到至少 20 個粒子才能使計數具有統計意義。

這對不同等級的含義：

  • Grade A（ISO 5，≥0.5µm，3,520 per m³）：Vs = 20/3,520 × 1000 ≈ 5.7 L。由於 Grade A 粒子極少，5.7 升就夠了。
  • Grade D（ISO 8，≥0.5µm，3,520,000 per m³）：Vs 更小，因粒子濃度高，少量樣本即可。

重點提示 — 最小採樣量 vs 連續監測的差異

ISO 14644-1 的最小採樣量是針對分類/資格確認用的——你要「宣告」這個房間是 ISO Class X，需要採多少樣本。

但日常生產監測（Routine EM）通常使用連續粒子計數器，每分鐘採集固定流量（通常 28.3 L/min = 1 CFM），這是一種不同的方法。兩者的目的不同：

  • ISO 採樣量（大）→ 用於「證明分類」（Classification/Qualification）
  • 連續監測（小流量但長時間）→ 用於「趨勢分析和即時警報」（Routine Monitoring）

PDA PtC-1 的立場：分類請遵守 ISO 14644-1，不要發明自己的採樣量——因為這是全球監管機構共同接受的標準。

公式 — ISO 14644-1 最小採樣量

最小採樣量計算：

Vs = (20 / Cn,m) × 1000  [單位：公升]

Cn,m = 該潔淨等級在目標粒徑下的最大濃度（per m³）

Grade A/B（ISO 5）：
  ≥0.5µm → Cn,m = 3,520 per m³
  → Vs = (20/3,520) × 1000 ≈ 5.67 L → 取整為 ≥ 6 L

Grade C（ISO 7）：
  ≥0.5µm → Cn,m = 352,000 per m³
  → Vs = (20/352,000) × 1000 ≈ 0.057 L ≈ 57 mL

Grade D（ISO 8）：
  ≥0.5µm → Cn,m = 3,520,000 per m³
  → Vs = (20/3,520,000) × 1000 ≈ 0.0057 L ≈ 5.7 mL

注意：實際取樣量通常遠大於最小值，
因連續粒子計數器每分鐘採 28.3L。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 Grade A 環境需要採集比 Grade C 更多體積的空氣樣本才能進行分類？這背後的統計學原理是什麼？
  2. 一個粒子計數器的流量為 28.3 L/min，每次採樣時間為 1 分鐘。這樣的採樣量對 Grade A 分類是否足夠？（請用計算說明。）
Topic O: ≥0.5 µm and ≥5 µm Total Particle Monitoring (p36–p37)

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement

Should limits be applied for ≥5 µm particle monitoring for Grade A routine monitoring?

Recommendation

Routine monitoring for ≥5 µm within Grade A can provide useful information. However, due to the low concentration of particles and the possibility of false readings, the setting of limits may be misleading. The focus should be on the overall trend rather than individual numbers, based on the low accuracy of the measurement when counting particles ≥5 µm separately. The analysis of monitoring-result trends is more appropriate.

Rationale

ISO 14644-1:2015 states:

"Sampling and statistical limitations for particles in low concentration make classification inappropriate… Sample collection limitations for both particles in low concentration and particles greater than 1 micrometer make classification of this particle size inappropriate, due to potential particle losses in the sampling system."

Monitoring and reporting of particles ≥0.5 µm and ≥5 µm should be adequate for evaluation of Grade A environments. However, limits are not required for ≥5 µm particles for Grade A classification purposes.

Footnote 1: Quantification of ≥5 µm particle monitoring for Grade A zones, in addition to ≥0.5 µm particle monitoring, is currently required by some regulatory agencies, including in the EU.

Footnote 2: The same recommendation should apply to Grade B environments in nonoperational (as-built/at-rest) conditions (ISO Class 5).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 為何 ≥5 µm 粒子監測如此困難？

粒子計數器（Particle Counter）是透過光散射原理偵測粒子。≥5 µm 的粒子計數面臨三個技術問題：

  • 濃度太低（Statistically Rare）：在 Grade A 環境中，≥5 µm 粒子本來就極少。當濃度極低時，計數的隨機誤差（統計誤差）相對於實際數字非常大——你可能測到 0、1、2 個粒子，但這個差異在統計上沒有意義。
  • 採樣管損失（Particle Loss in Tubing）：大粒子在彎曲的採樣管中容易沉降或撞壁損失，到達偵測器的粒子比實際少，造成「假低讀數」。
  • 假讀數（False Counts）：相反地，液滴（比如操作員呼吸或設備潤滑油霧）可能被誤計為大粒子，造成「假高讀數」。

ISO 14644-1 的結論是：≥5 µm 粒子計數的不確定性太高，不適合用於分類（Classification），但仍可用於趨勢監測。

比喻說明 — 在空蕩蕩的廣場數人頭

想像你需要計算一個巨大廣場上的人數。如果廣場上有 10,000 人（就像 Grade C 的粒子），計數誤差±100 人（1%）是可以接受的。

但如果廣場上只有 3 個人（Grade A 的 ≥5 µm 粒子），你的計數可能是 2 或 4 個人（±1 的誤差就是 33%！）。這個測量本身就不精確。

所以 PDA 說：在幾乎沒有 ≥5 µm 粒子的 Grade A 環境中，每次測到的個位數數字不應設定硬性限值——應該看的是「這個數字是否開始持續上升」（趨勢），而不是「這次測到了 2 個，超過了限值 1」。

重點提示 — PDA 與 EU Annex 1 的立場差異（監管現實）

這是 Topic O 最重要的監管張力：

機構 ≥5 µm Grade A 的要求
PDA PtC-1 建議監測但不建議設定硬性限值；使用趨勢分析
ISO 14644-1 認為 ≥5 µm 計數不適合用於分類（統計理由）
EU Annex 1 (2022) 要求定量監測並設定限值（Grade A：≥5 µm 最大 20 per m³）
FDA 沒有明確 ≥5 µm 的強制限值，傾向接受趨勢監測

CDMO 實務建議：如果你的產品在 EU 市場上市，EU Annex 1 要求優先——你必須設定並遵守 ≥5 µm 限值。同時在監測策略中說明你理解其統計局限性（引用 ISO 14644），並以趨勢分析作為補充解讀工具。這樣既滿足法規要求，又展現科學成熟度。

Grade A 粒子監測限值對照（EU Annex 1 2022）

EU Annex 1 (2022) Grade A 粒子限值：

狀態          ≥0.5 µm (per m³)    ≥5 µm (per m³)
At-Rest       3,520               20
In-Operation  3,520               20

Grade B：
狀態          ≥0.5 µm (per m³)    ≥5 µm (per m³)
At-Rest       3,520               29 (ISO 5 等效)
In-Operation  352,000             2,900

PDA PtC-1 的提醒：
對於 Grade A 的 ≥5 µm 限值（20 per m³），
由於測量不確定性，建議：
1. 遵守 EU 法規要求（必須測量並設定限值）
2. 同時做趨勢分析（不要過度解讀單次數字）
3. 假陽性出現時，優先排查液滴/油霧等假讀數來源
4. 建立查詢流程（Investigation Threshold）而非
   機械性地觸發生產停線

實務應用 — 如何處理 Grade A ≥5 µm 超標事件

假設你的 Grade A 充填區連續粒子監測器顯示 ≥5 µm 粒子突然從 0 變成 3 個（單次測量）。

根據 EU Annex 1 限值（20 per m³），3 個粒子是否需要啟動偏差調查？

PDA PtC-1 的建議思路：

  1. 首先核查是否為假讀數（液滴、油霧、儀器誤觸）
  2. 查看同時間的 ≥0.5 µm 數據是否也有異常（一致性驗證）
  3. 如果 ≥0.5 µm 正常而 ≥5 µm 偶發偏高，可能是假讀數——記錄並觀察趨勢
  4. 如果 ≥5 µm 持續升高或與 ≥0.5 µm 同步升高，啟動完整的偏差調查
  5. 調查焦點：是否有新污染源？設備維修後粒子未清除？

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. ISO 14644-1:2015 為什麼說 ≥5 µm 粒子計數「不適合用於分類」？其核心的科學理由是什麼？
  2. 你的設施同時面向 FDA 和 EMA 市場。針對 Grade A 的 ≥5 µm 監測，你的 EM 計畫應如何撰寫，才能同時滿足兩個監管機構的期望並展示科學成熟度？
  3. 為什麼 PDA PtC-1 在腳注中特別說明「Grade B 在 At-Rest 條件下（ISO Class 5）也應適用相同建議」？這個等同的依據是什麼？（提示：Grade B at-rest = ISO 5，與 Grade A in-operation 的粒子濃度相同。）

本節重點回顧 Section Summary — Topics I–O

  • 屏障技術層次（Topic I）：保護強度由低到高：傳統手工 < RABS（需 Grade B 環境）< Open Isolator（需 Grade C）< Closed Isolator（需 Grade D）。更高等級的屏障技術允許更低等級的周圍環境，從而降低廠房建造和運營成本。
  • 清除期以資格確認為準（Topic J）：EU Annex 1 的 20 分鐘是指引值，不是強制值。每個廠房應透過實測數據建立自己的清除期，重點在「確認粒子已恢復至 At-Rest 標準」，而非計時。
  • BFS 的特殊地位（Topic K.1–K.3）：BFS 因高度自動化和極短暴露時間，被允許在 Grade C 環境操作（不需 Grade B 過渡區），但充填關鍵區域仍需達到 Grade A 等效，並須透過資格確認（含煙霧可視化）證明。樹脂生物負荷和 APS 培養基可見度是 BFS 特有的管控挑戰。
  • 氣閘設計關鍵（Topic L）：最終更衣區應達到與通往區域相同等級的靜止條件；人員和物料氣閘應盡量分開；雙門滅菌器是物料無菌轉移的最優方案。
  • At-Rest vs In-Operation（Topic M）：兩種狀態都需要在資格確認中測試；日常生產監測只需 In-Operation；製程產生粒子（BFS、粉末充填）的環境應建立基準而非直接套用絕對限值。
  • 採樣量與粒子監測（Topic N, O）：分類採樣量依 ISO 14644-1 計算（最小 20 個粒子的統計量）；≥5 µm 粒子因統計局限性，PDA 建議趨勢分析而非硬性限值，但 EU Annex 1 要求設定限值——面向歐盟市場的廠房必須遵守，同時應用趨勢分析作為補充解讀工具。
2

Topic 2: II. Environmental Monitoring

II. 環境監控 | p37-p53

Section II: Environmental Monitoring PDA PtC-1 (2023)

環境監測（Environmental Monitoring）完整解析
PDA Points to Consider No. 1: Aseptic Processing (Revised 2023) | p37 – p53 | Topics A.1, B.1, C, D, E, F, G, H, I, J

本章學習目標 Learning Objectives

  • 理解警報水準（Alert Level）與行動限度（Action Limit）的本質差異，並能說明為何兩者均不等於產品規格（Specification）
  • 掌握 EU Annex 1 (2022) 對環境監測的新要求，包括 CCS 驅動的警報水準制定方法
  • 能設計涵蓋 Grade A/B/C/D 的 EM 監測計劃，包括地點、頻率、持續時間及取樣方式的風險決策
  • 了解 EM 超標事件的調查流程與記錄要求，以及對批次放行的影響評估
  • 掌握終端滅菌產品的房間分級需求、消毒劑輪替策略、環境菌株鑑定分級方案，以及培養基與培養條件的科學選擇

本節內容索引

A.1 設定警報/行動限度 B.1 EM 限度性質 C 批次放行關係 D 監測地點/頻率/持續時間 E 超標調查與記錄 F 終端滅菌產品分級 G 清潔消毒計劃 H 環境菌株鑑定 I 培養基生長促進測試 J 培養溫度
Topic A.1 — Setting Alert Levels and Action Limits | 設定警報水準與行動限度

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What are the recommended alert levels and action limits for aseptic processing areas?

Recommendation: Each manufacturer should have a formal program that stipulates the EM monitoring alert and action limits and the methods used to determine them. However, any contamination in a Grade A area (and in Grade B areas surrounding the Grade A area) or on product-contact surfaces should be investigated and the impact on any product batches should be assessed prior to batch release.

If new technologies are used for EM, the action limits for these methods should be at least comparable with the levels set for the established methods, with adjustments considered based on greater sensitivity of the new methods and agreed upon with regulators.

Alert levels should be based on historical data but should be lower than action limits so that it is possible to react before action limits are reached. PDA Technical Report No. 13 (Revised 2022) suggests statistical methods to be used for determination of alert levels.

For new facilities, production lines, or other aseptic processing areas where historical data are not available, alert levels can be based on similar aseptic processing areas within the facility or at another facility or can be established by use of environmental data generated during validation studies. In any of these situations, EM data from the new area are generated and should eventually be used to reset the alert levels.

Periodically thereafter, data should be reviewed and, if needed, alert levels may be adjusted (e.g., be made tighter or looser) based on the historical data. Caution should be used when limits are tightened to a level that approaches process capability. Alert limits that are significantly higher than trend data should also be avoided to ensure that a warning is triggered as soon as an abnormal situation occurs.

Rationale: Some agencies have published recommended action limits for conventional monitoring methods; such limits should be considered levels because they are not product specifications and may not be adequate for newer testing methods.

In general, as a company designs its EM program, alert and action limits should be determined on the basis of an assessment of product contamination risk that takes into consideration product and process characteristics, process robustness, level of gowning, historical data, and other information relevant to product contamination risk.

Not all situations require use of both alert and action limits; for example, it may not be possible to set alert levels for microorganisms in Grade A environments because any microorganisms present would require action.

"In general, EM trends are an important element in the evaluation of cleanroom performance. Due to the limited recovery capacity and the sampling nature of the methods, special attention should be given to the trends but without neglect of the single count result for the critical zones (Grade A or Grade B)."

Key References: EU Annex 1 (2022) | PDA TR-13 (Revised 2022) | PDA TR-59 (Statistical Methods) | USP <1116>

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 警報水準 vs 行動限度

Alert Level（警報水準）：根據歷史資料以統計方法設定的早期預警值。超過此值代表環境出現潛在不正常趨勢，需啟動調查，但不必然立即停止生產。

Action Limit（行動限度）：超過此值代表環境管控可能已失效，必須立即採取行動（CAPA），並評估對批次的影響。

重要原則：Alert Level 必須低於 Action Limit，才能在問題惡化至需要行動之前提供緩衝時間。

Grade A 特例：Grade A 區因任何微生物的存在都構成潛在風險，通常無法設定有意義的 Alert Level——任何菌落出現即觸發 Action 層級的回應。

比喻說明 — 警報與緊急疏散

想像一棟大樓的火災安全系統：

  • 煙霧偵測器響起（Alert Level）：某處有煙，保全人員前往確認，可能只是廚房蒸氣，但需要調查。大樓不需要立即疏散。
  • 灑水頭啟動（Action Limit）：確認有火災，立即啟動緊急疏散，同時保全介入處理。

EM 計劃的設計邏輯完全相同——建立「早期預警」讓你有時間反應，而不是等到問題失控才行動。

重點提示 — EU Annex 1 (2022) 新要求

EU Annex 1 2022 版本要求 Alert Level 的設定必須與設施的污染控制策略（CCS, Contamination Control Strategy）相連結。這意味著：

  • 不能只是照抄監管機關公佈的參考值
  • 必須根據自家設施的歷史數據、製程特性、屏障技術（RABS/Isolator）設計
  • 新設施可以用驗證數據或同類設施數據作為起始點，但必須定期根據實際數據更新

這是一個重大的思維轉變：從「達標」到「主動管理」。

統計方法設定 Alert Level（TR-13 建議）

常用方法（PDA TR-13 Revised 2022）：

方法一：均值 + 標準差法
  Alert Level = Mean + 3×SD（適用常態分佈資料）

方法二：百分位數法
  Alert Level = 95th 或 97.5th 百分位數
  （適用計數型資料，如 CFU）

方法三：上控制限（UCL）
  使用 Poisson 或負二項分佈計算
  適用於稀疏計數（多數值為零）的環境資料

設定原則：
  • 至少需要 30 個以上的資料點
  • 排除異常值（已確認調查的超標事件）
  • 定期重新評估（建議每年或累積足夠資料時）

實務應用 — CDMO 新廠設定情境

假設您的 CDMO 剛完成一條新的無菌充填線驗證，尚無歷史 EM 資料。依據 PtC-1 建議，您可以：

  1. 引用同廠區另一條已運作線的歷史均值作為起始 Alert Level
  2. 或使用驗證研究期間（至少 3 批 APS）收集的 EM 資料計算初始統計值
  3. 設定 6-12 個月的「磨合期」，持續收集數據後重新計算並更新
  4. 確保 Alert Level 遠低於 EU Annex 1 表格中的行動限度參考值

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果某 Grade B 監測點的歷史均值非常低（例如 0.1 CFU/m³），是否應該將 Alert Level 設為 0？這樣的設定有什麼實務問題？
  2. 引進新型即時微粒偵測技術（如 RMM）後，其 Action Limit 應如何與傳統培養法比較？
  3. 為什麼說「Alert Limit 顯著高於趨勢數據」也是需要避免的？
Topic B.1 — EM Alert and Action Limits: Not Specifications | EM 限度非產品規格

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: Should EM alert and action limits be considered specifications?

Recommendation: EM alert and action limits should not be considered specifications. However, any contamination in a Grade A or surrounding Grade B area or on product-contact surfaces should be investigated and the impact on any product batches should be assessed prior to batch release.

Rationale: Alert and action limits are used to monitor and control processes. Specifications relate to a direct measurement of product quality that is required to be met by an official monograph or filed application. Exceeding an alert or action limit does not produce an "out-of-specification" result.

However, any contamination in a Grade A area or on product-contact surfaces may be indicative of a potential product contamination and should be investigated, and the impact on any product batches should be thoroughly assessed prior to batch release.

EM alert and action limits are established for the purpose of detecting potential adverse changes or drifts in a validated aseptic processing environment. These levels are typically derived from historical data and are set conservatively. As such, alert and action limits are occasionally exceeded.

These situations provide early warning mechanisms that allow corrective actions to be taken before product quality is adversely affected. It is not appropriate to consider EM alert and action limits as extensions of product specifications because a cause-effect relationship does not automatically exist between EM level excursions and product contamination.

"This is evidenced by situations in which EM action limits are exceeded during zero-contamination-process simulations. Conversely, there are instances in which process simulation failures occur and no contamination is detected by EM."

Key References: PDA TR-13 (Revised 2022) | PDA TR-88 | USP <1116>

Recommended EU Annex 1 (2022) Grade Limits for Reference:

Grade Active Air Sampling (CFU/m³) Settle Plates 90mm, 4h (CFU/plate) Contact Plates 55mm (CFU/plate) Glove Print 5 fingers (CFU/glove)
A<1<1<1<1
B10555
C1005025—
D20010050—

Source: EU GMP Annex 1 (2022), Table 1. These are action limits for in-operation conditions. Alert levels are set separately by each facility based on historical data.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — EM 限度 vs 產品規格的根本差異

產品規格（Specification）：寫在 NDA/ANDA/MAA 等申請文件中，必須符合才能放行產品。超出即為 OOS（Out-of-Specification），觸發強制性調查程序，且通常導致批次拒絕。

EM 行動限度（Action Limit）：由廠商根據自身歷史數據設定的製程管控工具。超出觸發調查，但不自動等同於 OOS，也不必然導致批次拒絕。

關鍵邏輯：EM 超標 ≠ 產品污染。文件中明確指出：在 APS（無菌製程模擬）中可能出現 EM 超標但無培育失敗的情況，反之亦然。

比喻說明 — 交通警告標誌 vs 法律速限

EM 限度就像高速公路上的「建議速度」標誌（如「彎道建議時速 60km」）：超過它不一定違法，但代表潛在風險增加，應該放慢速度並調查原因。

產品規格則像法定速限：超過就是違規，無論其他情況如何，都會有法律後果。

混淆兩者的危險：若把 EM 限度當成規格，超標時就必須自動拒批，這會造成大量不必要的產品損失，且無法區分真正的品質風險與偶發的環境波動。

重點提示 — Grade A 超標：行動但非規格

Grade A 區任何微生物的存在（即便只有 1 CFU）雖然技術上不是「OOS」，但：

  • 必須進行完整調查
  • 必須評估對所有相關批次的影響
  • 批次放行決定需由 QP（歐盟）或負責人員基於調查結論做出
  • 單一 Grade A 超標不自動導致拒批，但調查結果若顯示製程失控，則必須拒批

這個「非規格但必須行動」的邏輯是無菌製造管控哲學的核心。

實務應用 — 批次放行決策情境

某批產品在充填期間，Grade B 空氣採樣結果為 12 CFU/m³（Action Limit = 10 CFU/m³）。此時：

  • 這不是 OOS，不觸發強制性 21 CFR 211.192 的 OOS 調查程序
  • 但必須啟動 EM 超標調查（偏差報告）
  • 調查需包含：菌株鑑定、HVAC 系統檢查、人員操作記錄、相鄰 Grade A 數據回顧
  • 若調查結論顯示無產品污染風險，批次可以在完整調查記錄的基礎上考慮放行

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. EM Action Limit 超標後，哪些情況下可以考慮放行批次？哪些情況下應該拒批？
  2. 如果一個 APS（媒體灌裝）出現培育失敗，但 EM 數據完全正常，這說明了什麼？應採取什麼行動？
  3. Grade A 的 Action Limit 為 <1 CFU/m³，如果檢測結果恰好是 1 CFU/m³，是否超標？
Topic C — EM Relationship to Batch Release | 環境監測與批次放行的關係

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What is the relationship between EM data from Grade A and Grade B areas and batch release?

Recommendation: Microbiological and particulate EM data generated in Grade A and Grade B environments should be reviewed as part of the batch-release process. Microbiological and particulate EM data from lower-grade areas may also be considered. EM results that exceed established action limits in Grade A and Grade B areas should be investigated and reviewed, and the risk to product safety should be evaluated.

A microbial count excursion of an established level, even in Grade A and Grade B zones, does not, by itself, mandate a batch rejection, provided that the investigation determines that there is no impact on product quality and safety. Excursions from action limits in lower-grade areas also require investigation, and this investigation may include impact on batch release.

Rationale: A carefully planned and executed EM program can provide a better understanding of the production environment. EM data are just one of many indicators used to evaluate an aseptic manufacturing process. Given the lack of accuracy and precision of a microbial count result, a single result alone may not be significant. However, any contamination in a Grade A and Grade B area or on product-contact surfaces should be investigated and the impact on any product batches should be assessed prior to batch release.

Reaching or exceeding an environmental action limit does not necessarily indicate that the product is adversely affected. An action-level excursion should precipitate an investigation. The overall purpose of the investigation is to determine the source of contamination and establish, insofar as possible, the cause-effect relationship between the observed action-level microbial count and cause(s) of product impact of the excursion.

The significance of an action-level excursion in EM and its impact on batch release is determined by a comprehensive investigation of all conditions that might impact the acceptability of the process and the batch(es) produced by that process.

Key References: PDA TR-13 (Revised 2022) | USP <71> | USP <1116>

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 風險導向的批次放行決策

PtC-1 明確採取風險導向（Risk-Based）立場：EM 超標本身不等同於批次拒絕。批次放行決策應基於完整調查的綜合判斷，而非單一數字。

必須納入批次放行審查的 EM 數據：

  • Grade A 和 Grade B 的微生物監測數據（強制性）
  • Grade A 和 Grade B 的微粒監測數據（強制性）
  • Grade C/D 數據（視情況考慮，非強制）

比喻說明 — 飛機黑盒子與事故調查

EM 數據就像飛機的飛行記錄器（黑盒子）：它記錄了飛行過程中的環境狀態，但黑盒子顯示某個瞬間的數據異常，不代表飛機一定墜毀了。

事故調查員需要結合黑盒子數據、機師報告、氣象記錄、機械檢查等所有資訊，才能得出最終結論。

同理，批次放行審查員需要結合 EM 數據、APS 記錄、人員操作日誌、維修記錄、菌株鑑定結果，才能做出科學決策。

重點提示 — 三種批次放行情境

情境一：EM 正常，無超標 → 常規批次放行審查，一般可放行。

情境二：Grade C/D 超標，Grade A/B 正常 → 啟動調查，評估根本原因；若調查顯示無產品影響，可考慮放行，但需完整記錄。

情境三：Grade A/B 超標 → 必須完整調查；若調查結論確認有產品污染風險（例如超標點直接鄰近開放容器），應考慮拒批或進行無菌性測試作為追加評估。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果批次放行時 EM 數據尚未完全取得（例如某些培養板仍在培養中），是否可以先放行？此時如何管理風險？
  2. 一個 Grade B 的 settle plate 顯示 6 CFU（Action Limit = 5 CFU），但 Grade A 數據完全正常，您會如何處理這個批次？
  3. 「原因-效果關係（cause-effect relationship）不自動存在」的邏輯，對 CDMO 的客戶溝通有何影響？如何向客戶解釋？
Topic D — Location, Frequency, and Duration of EM | 監測地點、頻率與持續時間

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What should the location, frequency, and duration of viable and total-particulate EM be in classified cleanroom areas?

NOTE: The principles presented in this topic are applicable to decision-making and criteria selection for EM conducted in cleanroom areas, including Grade A filling areas and adjacent support areas. These principles are applicable to various processing technologies, including conventional fill rooms, RABS, blow-fill-seal, and isolators.

Recommendation: The location, frequency, and duration of EM should be based on scientific analysis and risk-based decision-making.

  • The monitoring program should be designed to provide evidence of control within the environment without compromising the safety of the product, regardless of the technology used to maintain the environment. The monitoring method should capture data in a manner that is effective in determining environmental control. Trend analysis should be performed to assess the capability of contamination-control measures.
  • An understanding of the process and the inherent risk factors that can adversely affect product quality must exist. This includes selecting monitoring locations that will provide the best chance of detecting contamination in proximity to the product.

Companies should use risk assessment and analysis to determine which factors provide the needed information to make these decisions. Risk factors may include but are not necessarily limited to:

  • Frequency and duration of human activities in the monitored area
  • Efficiency of the barrier and other control systems designed to protect the product
  • Impact on the product of environment-borne contamination
  • Historical data related to process failures
  • Effectiveness of and risk associated with monitoring techniques
  • Regulatory and organizational commitments
  • Work (personnel, material, and process) flow
  • Airflow and differential pressure
  • Proximity to exposed components, products, or product-contact surfaces

NOTE: For more prescriptive criteria, practices, and requirements, see PDA TR-13.

  • The risk of performing the interventions associated with EM versus the benefit that EM information may provide should be considered. Location, frequency, and duration should be adequate to demonstrate control without the introduction of additional risk of microbial contamination by additional monitoring.
  • Duration is not a consideration for surface sampling; however, timing should be considered. Viable monitoring of sterilized product-contact surfaces should be performed only at the end of production.

Rationale: Although the Grade A and Grade B aseptic processing area is not sterile, well-controlled Grade A and Grade B conditions are an important factor in ensuring product sterility. Monitoring, although necessary to demonstrate control, also requires interventions that themselves present risk. Therefore, monitoring location, frequency, and duration must be carefully considered to optimize the benefit while the risk is managed.

Trend analysis is also recommended because of the inherent inaccuracy of any single microbiological EM result (i.e., colony-forming unit). Although a single microbial result may not be indicative of a problem, an adverse trend is much more likely to be an early warning of a potential degradation or loss of control within the environment.

The level of human activity and the potential risk of media residue needed to perform surface monitoring in the Grade A and Grade B environment pose a risk of contamination of products, components, and product-contact surfaces. Therefore, this activity should be performed at the completion of the aseptic process.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — EM 計劃設計的三大維度

1. 地點（Location）：應選在最可能偵測到污染的位置，且需最靠近產品暴露區。Grade A 的關鍵採樣點包括：充填針頭上方、容器開口上方、停機位置等。

2. 頻率（Frequency）：Grade A 需連續監測（微粒）；Grade B/C/D 頻率依風險評估決定。高風險操作（如人工介入）需增加臨時採樣。

3. 持續時間（Duration）：主動空氣採樣需定義取樣體積（通常 1 m³）；沉降碟有最長暴露時間限制（EU Annex 1 要求最多 4 小時）。表面採樣無持續時間概念，但時機（生產結束後）至關重要。

比喻說明 — Grade A 的 24 小時監視器

Grade A 的連續微粒監測就像監控攝影機（CCTV）：全程錄影，不是每小時才拍一張照片。

為什麼？因為污染事件往往是瞬間發生的（例如人員介入、設備故障），如果監測不連續，可能完全錯過最關鍵的時刻。

EU Annex 1 (2022) 進一步要求 Grade A 的微粒監測系統必須能夠實時（real-time）顯示並警報，而不只是事後讀取數據。

重點提示 — EM 介入本身是污染風險

這是一個容易被忽略的矛盾：為了證明環境受控，我們進行 EM；但 EM 的操作（人員進入、放置培養板、操作空氣採樣器）本身就是污染的來源。

實務應對：

  • Grade A 優先考慮無需人員介入的方法（如固定式連續微粒計數器）
  • 沉降碟暴露量（數量×時間）應最小化
  • 表面採樣應在充填完成後、滅菌前進行，不在充填過程中進行
  • 取樣動作應由訓練有素的人員以標準化方式執行，以降低操作引入的變異

沉降碟 vs 主動空氣採樣的比較

沉降碟（Settle Plate）：
  優點：簡單、成本低、可模擬粒子沉降到產品的風險
  缺點：無法定量（無採樣體積概念）
       長時間暴露有培養基乾燥問題
       EU Annex 1 限制最多 4 小時
  適用：作為主動採樣的補充，尤其是地面/工作台面評估

主動空氣採樣（Active Air Sampling）：
  優點：定量（CFU/m³）、時間彈性
  缺點：需要設備、採樣本身需人員操作
       流量和取樣體積影響回收率
  適用：Grade A/B 定量微生物監測主要方法

Grade A 要求：連續微粒監測（≥0.5 µm 和 ≥5.0 µm）
              微生物採樣每批次或每操作段

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 使用隔離器（Isolator）進行無菌充填時，EM 計劃的設計與使用 RABS 有何不同？哪些監測點可以省略或調整？
  2. 如果一條充填線一天生產三個班次，Grade B 的 EM 應以何種頻率採樣才算足夠？
  3. 為什麼表面採樣必須在「生產結束後」而非「生產過程中」進行？如果違反這個原則會有什麼風險？
Topic E — Investigation and Documentation of EM Excursions | 超標調查與記錄

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: How should EM excursions be investigated and documented?

Recommendation: Elements to include in the investigation depend on the sample type where the action-level excursion occurred. Suggestions on which elements to include in the investigation can be found in PDA TR-13. The corrective and preventive actions must be documented and kept as GMP documentation for investigations in relation to exceeding action limits. Additional details on investigation elements can be found in PDA Technical Report No. 88.

Records should be maintained as part of the routine EM program, including results for samples exceeding action limits and include:

  • Description of the deficiency
  • Possible causes
  • Action steps and their schedule for implementation
  • Identification of persons responsible for relevant corrective action
  • Evaluation of effectiveness of action steps

Evaluation of trends of the sample location and adjacent room/area and microbial excursion identification results should be included and documented in the investigation.

The risk for product safety must be evaluated for EM results exceeding action limits in Grade A and Grade B. The investigation should include product impact assessment and evaluate the risk to other products manufactured in the same time frame.

Rationale: EM is a critical element of the sterility assurance program and is one of the most important measures of control in clean areas. It provides meaningful information on the quality of the environment and should promptly identify potential routes of contamination, allowing for corrective action to prevent product contamination.

The documentation is used for recording and demonstrating that the environment has been in control during production of products, and also that the impact on product quality has been evaluated. Furthermore, the documentation should be used for checking the effectiveness of the corrective and preventive actions taken by reviewing previous investigations for similar occurrences.

Key References: EU Annex 1 (2022) | ISO 13408-1 | PDA TR-13 (Revised 2022) | PDA TR-88 | FDA Aseptic Processing Guidance (2004)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — EM 超標調查的五個核心要素

PtC-1 列出的調查記錄要素，對應了 GMP 調查的標準架構：

  1. 問題描述（What）：哪個採樣點，哪種方法，結果數值
  2. 可能原因（Why）：根本原因分析（RCA），使用魚骨圖等工具
  3. 行動計劃（How）：CAPA 清單，包含責任人和完成時限
  4. 責任人（Who）：每個行動步驟均有指定負責人
  5. 有效性評估（Does it work?）：CAPA 完成後的追蹤驗證

比喻說明 — EM 超標調查決策樹

想像 EM 超標調查就像醫師的診斷流程：

  • 症狀出現（超標數據）→ 先排除假陽性（採樣錯誤？培養問題？）
  • 初步評估 → 超標發生在哪個 Grade？哪個時間點？
  • 鑑別診斷 → 菌株鑑定：是皮膚菌（人員）？水菌（管路）？孢子菌（環境持久性問題）？
  • 病因追蹤 → 查閱當日操作日誌、HVAC 記錄、人員 gowning 記錄
  • 治療方案 → CAPA：清潔消毒加強、人員培訓、設備維修
  • 康復追蹤 → 後續 EM 數據確認 CAPA 有效

重點提示 — 調查的時間性與範圍延伸

時間性：EM 超標調查不能只看發現超標的那一個時間點。需要回顧相鄰批次、相鄰時段的趨勢，以確認是偶發事件還是系統性問題。

空間延伸：Grade A/B 超標時，必須評估對同一時間段在該設施生產的其他批次（包括不同產品）的影響。

GMP 文件要求：調查報告必須是正式的 GMP 記錄，可供監管機構審查。不充分的調查記錄是 FDA 483 觀察項目的常見來源。

實務應用 — 調查報告的常見缺失（FDA 483 觀察項目）

  • 根本原因分析不足（僅記錄「偶發事件」，未深入探討）
  • CAPA 缺乏具體時限和責任人
  • 未評估對同期生產批次的影響
  • 未追蹤 CAPA 的有效性（無 follow-up EM 數據）
  • 趨勢分析缺失（未與歷史數據比較）

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在 EM 調查中發現超標菌株為 Bacillus 孢子菌（難以被一般消毒劑殺滅），您的 CAPA 計劃應包含哪些特殊措施？
  2. 如果相同採樣點連續三次超標，根本原因調查的重點應從哪裡著手？
  3. EM 超標事件發生在週五下午，批次準備週一放行。您需要在週末完成哪些評估才能做出放行決定？
Topic F — Room Classification for Terminally Sterilized Products | 終端滅菌產品的房間分級

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What is the appropriate cleanliness grade for areas used in the manufacturing of terminally sterilized liquid products?

Recommendation:

  • A Grade D environment or better is typically suitable for the control of environmental microbiological risks during compounding of a terminally sterilized product formulation as long as microbial ingress and growth risks at this stage of manufacturing are properly mitigated.
  • A Grade C environment or better is typically suitable for the control of environmental microbiological risks during the filling of terminally sterilized liquid product formulations as long as microbial ingress and growth risks are properly mitigated at this stage of manufacture.
  • Based on risk assessment and historical data, higher environmental classifications may be required for compounding and filling operations.

The compounding and solution transmission system should be a closed system (the compounding portion open to the environment only when actively adding ingredients), thereby minimizing the potential for ingress of microorganisms into the process stream.

Rationale: The manufacturing process for terminally sterilized solution products typically consists of:

  1. Compounding of pharmaceutical ingredients in WFI to appropriate formulation requirements
  2. Filtration of solution (0.45 μm or better)
  3. Filling and sealing of solution into the container–closure system
  4. Terminal sterilization (PNSU ≤10⁻⁶) of the solution and container–closure system

The greatest microbiological risks for this process include:

  1. Ingress of microorganisms into the process through WFI and other raw-material ingredients
  2. Ingress of microorganisms into the compounding system
  3. Growth of microorganisms in the aqueous formulation during the time between compounding and terminal sterilization
  4. Ingress of microorganisms into the product during filling
  5. Ingress of microorganisms into the product from microorganisms resident on the container–closure system

A microbial retentive filter (0.45 μm or 0.2 μm) should be used prior to filling as a critical control point. An active filter-integrity testing program must be in effect with passing integrity results a critical requirement for product release.

Microbiological testing should be performed upstream of the microbial retentive filter and also on filled containers (presterilized product bioburden) immediately prior to exposure to the terminal sterilization process.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 終端滅菌 vs 無菌充填的環境要求差異

無菌充填（Aseptic Filling）：無滅菌步驟補救，充填區需要 Grade A 環境，對 EM 有最嚴格要求。

終端滅菌（Terminal Sterilization）：最後一道滅菌步驟（PNSU ≤10⁻⁶）提供了強大的安全網，因此充填區僅需 Grade C（通常），配製區僅需 Grade D。

但仍需管控！原因：如果充填前的生物負荷（Bioburden）過高，即使 D-value 正常的高壓滅菌也可能無法達到 PNSU ≤10⁻⁶，尤其對耐熱孢子菌而言。

比喻說明 — 微波爐重新加熱 vs 無菌手術

終端滅菌就像用微波爐重新加熱食物：即使準備過程不夠乾淨，最終加熱步驟可以殺死大多數細菌。但如果食物已經腐爛到極點（生物負荷極高），微波爐也無法完全補救。

無菌充填就像外科手術：整個過程必須維持無菌，因為沒有最後一道「滅菌」步驟可以補救任何失誤。

這就是為什麼終端滅菌產品的環境要求雖然不如無菌充填嚴格，但仍然需要系統性的微生物管控。

重點提示 — 生物負荷管控是關鍵防線

對終端滅菌產品而言，生物負荷（Bioburden）測試是最重要的製程管控指標之一：

  • 必須在過濾器之前（upstream）和充填後（presterilized）兩個點測試
  • Action Limit 的設定需與滅菌週期設計相符
  • 耐熱孢子數量（moist-heat-resistant spore count）需特別關注
  • 配製到滅菌之間的時間（hold time）需有最大時限，超過需重新評估
  • 過濾器完整性測試（IFT/FFT）是批次放行的關鍵條件

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果終端滅菌產品的充填線安裝在一個 Grade B 環境中（比要求更嚴格），這有什麼商業利弊？
  2. 滅菌前生物負荷超出 Action Limit 時，是否可以延長滅菌時間來補救？這樣做有什麼風險？
  3. 配製用水（WFI）的微生物控制為什麼對終端滅菌產品特別重要？
Topic G — Cleaning and Disinfection Program for Grade A and B | 清潔與消毒計劃

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: How is a cleaning and disinfection program for a Grade A and Grade B room designed and qualified?

Recommendation: A disinfection program for Grade A and Grade B rooms should be designed to achieve an acceptable level of decontamination.

The disinfection program should be designed based on a risk assessment that includes consideration of the following:

  • Cleaning of surfaces within the Grade A and Grade B rooms is a prerequisite for effective disinfection
  • Disinfectant should be capable of achieving a 2 log reduction for bacterial spores, 3 log reduction for vegetative/fungi to a spectrum of microbial flora (including site isolates) on representative surfaces
  • Disinfecting procedure should be capable of achieving not less than a 1 log reduction of bacterial spores or vegetative/fungi in a 1–5 minute contact time
  • Chemical compatibility with the surfaces
  • Effectiveness on different surfaces taking into account surface characteristics and necessary dwell time, wetting time, or contact time; this should be confirmed with in-house studies against actual surfaces using the actual application process in each facility and may be supplemented with reference to vendor literature
  • Feasibility and safety of application
  • Efficacy and reproducibility of the application procedure
  • Potential disinfectant residues
  • Procedures defined in sufficient detail about the sequence and specific locations to be disinfected and the detailed disinfection records (e.g., logbooks)

Initial qualification typically includes the actual disinfection process, including the maximum time between disinfections, followed by more intensive environmental sampling.

EM evaluates the efficacy of the disinfection program in an ongoing manner. The EM program should include trend analysis and periodic evaluation of changes in the environmental flora.

Rationale: A disinfection program is dependent on a combination of the disinfecting chemicals selected, the physical surfaces to be disinfected, the cleaning of the physical surfaces, and the reproducibility of the disinfectant application process.

Caution should be used when employing a vigorous wiping application during the validation of the effectiveness of the disinfectant agent because the wiping action may enhance the removal of contaminating entities.

Key References: EU Annex 1 (2022) | PDA TR-13 (Revised 2022) | PDA TR-70 | FDA Aseptic Processing Guidance | USP <1072>

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 消毒計劃的層次架構

第一層：清潔（Cleaning） — 必須先清潔才能有效消毒。有機物（蛋白質、油脂）會保護微生物免受消毒劑作用。

第二層：一般消毒劑（General Disinfectant） — 殺滅蔬菌（Vegetative bacteria）和真菌，如 70% 異丙醇（IPA）、季銨鹽（Quats）。

第三層：孢子殺滅劑（Sporicide） — 殺滅 Bacillus 等孢子菌，如過氧化氫（H₂O₂）氣體、過氧乙酸（Peracetic acid）。EU Annex 1 (2022) 明確要求 Grade A/B 必須定期使用孢子殺滅劑。

比喻說明 — 消毒劑輪替如同抗生素輪替

長期使用同一種消毒劑，環境中的微生物可能逐漸產生適應性或耐受性（雖然與抗生素耐藥機制不完全相同，但同樣的後果：效力降低）。

就像醫院的感染管控計劃會輪替使用不同抗生素來避免耐藥菌的產生，無菌製造設施也應定期輪替不同類別的消毒劑，確保廣譜有效性。

EU Annex 1 (2022) 明確規定消毒劑輪替的概念，並要求每種消毒劑均需進行有效性驗證（對場地分離菌株的驗證尤為重要）。

重點提示 — EU Annex 1 (2022) 對消毒的新要求

EU Annex 1 (2022) 相比舊版有幾個重要的清潔消毒新要求：

  • 孢子殺滅劑（Sporicide）必須定期使用於 Grade A 和 Grade B，不再只是「建議」
  • 消毒劑必須針對設施自身的環境菌株（site isolates）進行有效性驗證，不能只依賴通用數據
  • 消毒劑的有效性必須與 CCS（污染控制策略）整合考量
  • 對消毒後的接觸時間（contact time/dwell time）需明確規定並遵守

消毒效力要求總結

PtC-1 消毒劑效力最低要求：

對細菌孢子（Bacterial Spores）：
  ≥ 2 log 殺滅（在代表性表面）
  ≥ 1 log 殺滅（在 1-5 分鐘接觸時間內）

對蔬菌和真菌（Vegetative bacteria & Fungi）：
  ≥ 3 log 殺滅（在代表性表面）
  ≥ 1 log 殺滅（在 1-5 分鐘接觸時間內）

驗證對象必須包含：
  ✓ 法定標準菌株（Compendial organisms）
  ✓ 設施自身分離菌株（Site isolates）
  ✓ 設施實際使用的表面材質
  ✓ 設施實際的應用程序（抹布/噴霧/泡沫）

注意：過度用力的擦拭動作可能誇大消毒劑效力
（PtC-1 明確警告）

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您設施的 EM 趨勢顯示 Grade B 出現 Bacillus 孢子菌的比例升高，您會如何調整消毒計劃？
  2. 消毒劑驗證通常使用供應商提供的數據是否足夠？PtC-1 對此有何立場？
  3. 如果清潔人員在擦拭消毒時用力過猛（vigorous wiping），驗證數據會如何受影響？這對設定例行操作規程有何啟示？
Topic H — Identification of Environmental Isolates | 環境菌株鑑定策略

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What microbial identification strategy is appropriate for the EM of samples?

Recommendation: The characterization, identification, strain typing, potential source, and cause of microorganisms recovered from environmental and personnel monitoring are important parts of surveillance programs. The characterization and identification program selected by the laboratory should be defined in writing.

This written description should specify:

  • The frequency of characterization and identification
  • The standard procedures for the methods used
  • The consistency with regulatory expectations for identification

A characterization beyond the species level, a comparison of microorganism identification profiles, and the creation of a user-database may be useful in tracking and evaluating monitoring trends.

Table H-1 gives an example of a scheme for the extent of characterization that may be used for the recovered microbial isolates:

Isolate and Origin Extent of Identification/Characterization (Minimum Expectations)
Environmental monitoring of Grade C and D classification areas for alert-level excursions Characterization (Gram stain reaction and morphology) only
Environmental monitoring for action-level excursions for Grade C and Grade D classification areas Identification to species level
Grade A and Grade B classification areas and alert- and/or action-level isolates from excipient, finished product, environment, and water samples Identification to species level
Significant product or process contamination failure (e.g., media fills or sterility tests) and significant adverse trends in environment and water monitoring Identification to strain level using such methods as strain typing, molecular fingerprinting (genotypic method), riboprinting

NOTE: Care should be used in comparisons of results from different identification methods.

NOTE: As noted in EU Annex 1, "Consideration should also be given to the identification of microorganisms detected in grade C and D areas (for example where action limits or alert levels are exceeded) or following the isolation of organisms that may indicate a loss of control, deterioration in cleanliness or that may be difficult to control such as spore-forming microorganisms and moulds and at a sufficient frequency to maintain a current understanding of the typical flora of these areas."

Rationale: Characterizations can be useful clues to the possible source of isolates. For example, Staphylococcus species are commonly found on skin, and Pseudomonas species are usually associated with water.

A change in the microbial flora might signify a change in a system that should be investigated. Initially, many isolates may be characterized and identified to establish a database of the microorganisms found in the area. Periodic identifications should be performed on routine monitoring to check for changes in predominant groups of microflora.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 鑑定層次與觸發條件

Table H-1 建立了一個「比例原則」的鑑定策略——分析深度與風險程度相匹配：

  • 形態學（Gram stain + 菌落形態）：Grade C/D 警報水準超標的初步篩選
  • 菌種鑑定（Species level）：Grade C/D 行動限度超標；Grade A/B 的任何超標；水及賦形劑的超標
  • 菌株鑑定（Strain level）：重大失敗事件（APS 失敗、無菌性測試失敗）；顯著不良趨勢

菌株鑑定方法包括：脈衝場膠電泳（PFGE）、MALDI-TOF MS、16S rRNA 定序、全基因組定序（WGS）。

比喻說明 — 警方犯罪調查的層次

菌株鑑定就像警方的犯罪偵查：

  • 形態學 = 目擊者描述（「高個子男性」）：快速粗略，無法確認身份
  • 菌種鑑定 = 照片比對（「和嫌疑人同類型外觀」）：更精確，但仍可能有多人符合
  • 菌株鑑定 = DNA 指紋比對：可確認「就是這個人」，並追溯來源

當 APS 失敗或產品無菌性測試失敗時，必須進行「DNA 指紋比對」（菌株鑑定），才能確認污染源並設計精準 CAPA。

重點提示 — 建立設施菌株資料庫

為什麼要建立 user-database（設施菌株資料庫）？

  • 了解設施的「正常菌相」（typical flora），才能偵測到異常
  • 新菌種出現 → 可能有新的污染源（新原材料、新人員、施工等）
  • 特定菌株反覆出現 → 提示設施中存在持續性污染點（niche/reservoir）
  • 消毒後孢子菌比例上升 → 提示消毒計劃對孢子菌效力不足

EU Annex 1 (2022) 新增要求：即使是 Grade C/D 的正常監測（非超標），也應定期進行菌株鑑定以建立並維護菌相理解。

常見環境菌株與污染源指示關係

菌種 → 典型來源 / 意義

Staphylococcus spp.   → 人員皮膚 / gowning 失效
Micrococcus spp.      → 人員皮膚、毛髮
Bacillus spp.         → 環境孢子 / 消毒劑效力不足
Aspergillus spp.      → 空氣（過濾器失效？）/ 外部帶入
Pseudomonas spp.      → 水系統 / 表面潮濕點
Burkholderia spp.     → 水系統 / 消毒劑污染
Penicillium spp.      → 原材料 / 外包裝帶入
Candida spp.          → 人員皮膚 / 黏膜

關鍵原則：
菌種鑑定提供「來源假說」，需結合
現場調查（操作記錄、設備狀態、物料來源）
才能確認根本原因。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. APS（媒體灌裝）出現一個培育失敗，分離到 Staphylococcus epidermidis，同時 EM 數據正常。您的調查重點應集中在哪裡？
  2. 如果 Grade B 監測連續三個月都出現 Pseudomonas 菌，但每次都在 Action Limit 以下，這代表什麼？應採取什麼行動？
  3. MALDI-TOF MS 與傳統生化鑑定方法在結果比較上有什麼注意事項？（提示：PtC-1 中有相關警語）
Topic I — Growth-Promotion Testing of EM Media | 培養基生長促進測試

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What constitutes a scientifically appropriate program for routine growth promotion testing of EM media?

Recommendation: A quality management program for all incoming or in-house prepared media should be in place for evaluating media for its intended use and for its acceptance. Lots of media should be tested for their ability to reliably recover microorganisms. The growth-promotion test is one of the tests conducted by the microbiology laboratory that is used to achieve this.

For growth-promotion testing of media used for EM, there should be a predefined list of test organisms. This list should include:

  • Compendial organisms (required)
  • Environmental isolates if those isolates differ materially from compendial microorganisms (may be included)
  • A range of "representative" microorganisms that could be encountered in manufacturing environments (e.g., Gram-positive rod; Gram-positive coccus; filamentous mold and yeast; Gram-negative rod)

Growth-promotion testing may also demonstrate that the transportation route and different processing methods do not adversely impact the ability of the media to recover microorganisms.

Skip-lot testing, in which not all of the lots are tested, might be justified based on consideration of risk elements, including but not limited to:

  • A robust supplier quality system
  • Audit program
  • Communication/notification policy
  • Experience with the vendor

Rationale: EM media should have demonstrated the capability to recover a range of potential microbial contaminants.

Key References: USP <61> | USP <71> | USP <1116> | USP <1227>

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 培養基本身也需要品質管控

EM 結果的可靠性完全依賴培養基的品質。如果培養基無法有效回收微生物，則所有 EM 數據都是虛假的安全感。

Growth-Promotion Test（生長促進測試）的目的：確認培養基能夠支持目標微生物的生長，且回收率符合要求（通常為 70%-200% 的接種量回收，或 USP 要求的計數標準）。

測試時機：

  • 每個新批號（lot）收貨時
  • 供應商允許的情況下可進行 Skip-lot testing
  • 運輸後（如懷疑溫度超標）
  • 媒體製備後（in-house 製備）

比喻說明 — 培養基就像偵測器的電池

想像您的 EM 計劃是一個火災偵測系統，培養基就是偵測器裡的電池。如果電池沒電（培養基失效），偵測器永遠不會響——不是因為沒有火災，而是因為偵測器根本無法工作。

定期的 Growth-Promotion Test 就是「定期更換電池並測試偵測器功能」，確保 EM 系統處於功能性狀態。

重點提示 — Skip-Lot Testing 的合理化

並非每一個批號都必須進行 100% 的 GPT。PtC-1 允許在以下條件下進行 Skip-lot testing（部分批次測試）：

  • 供應商有健全的品質體系（QMS）
  • 定期對供應商進行稽核
  • 有效的溝通/通知政策（供應商必須主動通知任何製造變更）
  • 有長期良好的供應商使用記錄

風險管控：即使進行 Skip-lot，仍需要統計計劃（如每 N 批測試一批）並記錄合理化依據。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果 GPT 結果顯示某批培養基的回收率偏低（例如只有 50%），已經用這批培養基採集的 EM 樣品結果應如何處理？
  2. 除了法定標準菌株（Compendial organisms），為什麼可能需要加入設施自身分離菌株進行 GPT？
  3. 培養基從供應商到使用之間的運輸過程（transportation route）可能造成哪些問題？如何驗證？
Topic J — Incubation Temperatures for EM Samples | EM 樣品培養溫度

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What incubation conditions are scientifically appropriate for EM samples?

Recommendation: Mesophilic incubation conditions (a single temperature within the range of 20°C to 35°C ± 2.5°C for three to seven days) are suitable for recovery of microorganisms from normal ambient-temperature manufacturing environments.

Although detection of yeasts and molds can be improved by the use of specialized recovery media, a nonselective microbiological growth medium, such as casein soybean digest agar (or soybean casein digest agar (SCDA)), is suitable in most cases for the total aerobic flora.

Assessment of environmental isolates and the incubation temperature regimen is recommended to confirm that the use of the nonselective media is sufficient to address the risk posed by any unique conditions in a particular cleanroom environment.

Each manufacturer should select appropriate media and incubation regimens. The media used by various monitoring methods should be exposed and incubated according to the established EM program, and growth-promotion tests should be conducted using compendial standard organisms; these tests may include environmental isolates.

NOTE: Some studies have shown that recovery of yeast and mold may be hampered by incubation at higher temperatures (above 30°C), but scientific consensus has not yet been established.

Rationale: There is no universal set of incubation conditions that will reliably detect all types of environmental microorganisms that could be present from a given sampling site at a given point in time.

The use of a non-selective medium should be sufficient to achieve this objective. An assessment of environmental isolates should be performed to confirm that the use of the nonselective medium is sufficient to address the risk posed by any unique conditions in a particular cleanroom environment.

The recovery of environmental molds should be considered in the selection of the incubation temperature range and sequence of incubation temperatures, with a procedure and frequency based on risk assessment.

Key References: PDA TR-13 (Revised 2022) | PDA TR-22 (Revised 2011) | USP <1116>

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 為什麼培養溫度有爭議？

不同的微生物有不同的最適生長溫度：

  • 嗜溫菌（Mesophiles）如大多數細菌：最適 30-37°C
  • 嗜冷菌（Psychrotrophs）如某些環境菌：最適 20-25°C
  • 酵母菌和黴菌：最適 22-25°C，高溫（>30°C）可能抑制生長

PtC-1 的立場：單一溫度（20-35°C 範圍內任何一點）對大多數製造環境已足夠，但需要根據設施的環境菌相評估是否需要雙溫培養。

比喻說明 — 雙溫培養 vs 單溫培養

培養溫度的選擇就像設定食物保存溫度：

如果你只用 37°C 的溫箱培養，就像只在夏天（高溫）測試食品安全——會看到嗜溫菌，但可能錯過在 4°C 冰箱中也能生長的嗜冷菌。

EU Annex 1 歷史上建議雙溫培養（20-25°C 培養後再 30-35°C），以確保同時捕捉酵母/黴菌和細菌。PtC-1 採取更靈活的立場——只要科學評估支持，單一溫度也可以接受。

重點提示 — EU Annex 1 (2022) 與 PDA PtC-1 的異同

EU Annex 1 (2022) 立場：推薦雙溫培養（先 20-25°C 培養約 5 天，再 30-35°C 培養約 2 天），以確保黴菌和細菌均被有效回收。這是一個更保守的方法。

PDA PtC-1 立場：認為單一溫度在大多數情況下已足夠，但需要科學評估支持。採用非選擇性培養基（如 SCDA）在 20-35°C 之間的任一溫度培養 3-7 天，是科學上合理的。

實務建議：如果您的產品在歐盟市場銷售，建議採用 EU Annex 1 的雙溫培養方案，以滿足監管預期。

培養條件設計決策框架

步驟一：了解設施環境菌相
  → 對現有 EM 分離菌株進行溫度耐受性評估
  → 查看歷史數據：是否有酵母/黴菌超標？

步驟二：選擇培養基
  → SCDA（Soybean Casein Digest Agar）= 最通用選擇
  → Sabouraud Dextrose Agar（SDA）= 若需強化酵母/黴菌回收

步驟三：選擇培養條件
  選項A（PDA TR-13 / USP 建議）：
    30-35°C × 3-5 天（細菌優先）
    + 20-25°C × 5-7 天（酵母/黴菌）

  選項B（EU Annex 1 2022）：
    先 20-25°C × ~5 天 → 再 30-35°C × ~2 天

  選項C（單一溫度，需科學評估支持）：
    22-25°C × 5-7 天

步驟四：生長促進測試（GPT）驗證所選條件
  → 確認所選培養基+溫度能回收目標菌株

實務應用 — CDMO 客戶監管市場差異

CDMO 通常同時服務多個市場的客戶。以 EM 培養溫度為例：

  • 美國 FDA 市場：USP <1116> 允許靈活的培養條件，科學評估支持即可
  • 歐盟 EMA 市場：EU Annex 1 (2022) 傾向雙溫培養，監查員可能期待看到
  • 日本 PMDA 市場：JPE 與 USP 接近，但監查員有時有更嚴格的期待

建議：在驗證階段就建立能滿足最嚴格要求的培養條件（EU Annex 1），並在法規文件中說明選擇依據，以應對多市場客戶的需求。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您設施的歷史 EM 數據顯示從未分離到黴菌，是否可以用這個理由省略低溫培養？您需要什麼數據來支持這個決定？
  2. 如果培養時間從 5 天縮短至 3 天，可能會錯過哪些類型的微生物？在什麼情況下這樣的縮短是合理的？
  3. 非選擇性培養基（Nonselective media）的優點和缺點各是什麼？什麼情況下應該考慮使用選擇性培養基？

本節重點回顧 Section II Summary

  • Alert Level vs Action Limit：兩者均非產品規格（Specification）；Alert Level 基於統計/歷史數據，需低於 Action Limit；Grade A 通常無 Alert Level（任何菌落均需行動）。EU Annex 1 (2022) 要求警報水準設定需與 CCS 整合。
  • EM 與批次放行：Grade A/B 的 EM 數據必須納入批次放行審查；超標不自動等同於拒批，但必須完整調查並評估產品影響。風險導向決策是核心原則。
  • 監測計劃設計（地點/頻率/持續時間）：需基於風險評估，Grade A 需連續微粒監測；EM 本身也帶來介入風險，需平衡監測效益與操作風險；表面採樣必須在生產結束後進行。
  • EM 超標調查：必須包含根本原因分析、CAPA（含責任人和時限）、產品影響評估、趨勢分析和 CAPA 有效性追蹤。調查記錄是正式 GMP 文件。
  • 終端滅菌產品：配製區 Grade D、充填區 Grade C 通常已足夠，但生物負荷管控（包括過濾前和充填後的 Bioburden 測試）是關鍵安全防線。
  • 清潔消毒：EU Annex 1 (2022) 要求 Grade A/B 定期使用孢子殺滅劑；消毒劑有效性必須針對設施自身菌株驗證；消毒劑應輪替使用；清潔是消毒的前提。
  • 環境菌株鑑定：Table H-1 的分級鑑定策略——從形態學到菌株分型，深度與風險相匹配；建立設施菌株資料庫是追蹤菌相變化的基礎工具。
  • 培養基 GPT：每批培養基需通過生長促進測試；測試菌株需包含法定標準菌株並可加入設施環境菌株；Skip-lot testing 在滿足條件下可以接受。
  • 培養溫度：20-35°C 範圍內的單一溫度培養在大多數情況下已科學合理；EU Annex 1 (2022) 傾向雙溫（20-25°C 先行後 30-35°C）以強化酵母/黴菌回收；選擇需要根據設施菌相評估支持。
3a

Topic 3a: III. Validation/APS (A-H): Acceptance Criteria & Design

III. 驗證/APS(A-H)：接受標準與設計 | p54-p65

Section III: Validation — Aseptic Process Simulation (APS) Topics A–H

第三章：驗證 — 無菌製程模擬主題 A 至 H
PDA Points to Consider No. 1: Aseptic Processing (Revised 2023) | p54 – p65
A: Acceptance Criteria 驗收標準 B: Duration 時程長度 C: Incubation Temperatures 培養溫度 D: Nonintegral & Rejected Units 非完整容器 E: Reconciliation 核對計算 F: Inversion 倒置操作 G: Aerobic vs Anaerobic 好氧 vs 厭氧 H: APS Boundaries 範圍界定

本章學習目標

  • 理解 APS（Aseptic Process Simulation，無菌製程模擬）驗收標準的統計學基礎，以及「零汙染」目標背後的監管邏輯
  • 能夠設計符合生產最差狀況的 APS 執行時間，理解「事件驅動」而非「時間驅動」的原則
  • 解釋雙溫培養（20–25°C + 30–35°C）的科學理由，並能判斷何時採用單一溫度
  • 辨別哪些容器應納入培養（含宇宙組、cosmetic 缺陷組），哪些可合理排除（破損/非完整），並掌握核對（Reconciliation）計算
  • 理解 APS 範圍的起訖點：從滅菌後組件到最終容器密封；PUPSIT 須納入 APS
  • 說明為何好氧培養基（如 SCDA）足以應對大多數製程，以及採用厭氧培養的罕見例外
Topic A: Acceptance Criteria — 驗收標準

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What are the acceptance criteria for aseptic process simulations?

Recommendation: The objective of APS is to produce zero contaminated units, irrespective of run size. Therefore, the target involving such simulations should be zero positive units.

Upon discovery of any positive units, an investigation that includes a comprehensive risk assessment should be performed to assess any potential root causes, implementation of corrective and preventive actions (CAPA), and respective documentation.

In addition to other qualification requirements, it may be advisable to include multiple process-simulation runs to verify the robustness of the implemented corrective actions with consideration of the following:

  • Potential for multiple root causes
  • Unintended consequences inherently introduced by CAPAs that are otherwise not sufficiently challenged, or that may represent a departure from the original qualified state

Investigations that determine a definitive and readily identifiable root cause might provide grounds for a reduced number of repeat run(s). However, CAPAs should be put in place to avoid such issues and prevent deviations to studies and processes from reoccurring.

In all cases, the execution of additional run(s) without the undertaking of a comprehensive risk-based investigation to identify and correct any potential root causes is not acceptable.

Rationale: Process simulation contamination rates resulting in zero positive units should be achievable in well-designed and well-operated production lines.

The APS provides additional, but not absolute, assurance of process control on a periodic basis. While part of the overall approach to process validation, process simulation is only one of the many tools or approaches designed to evaluate the processing steps for aseptic manufacture.

The necessarily high degree of control and assurance for aseptic processes relies collectively on the qualification and validation of many systems, including product, equipment and component sterilization, personnel training and aseptic behavior, and environmental controls, and extends to facility design, inclusive of personnel, material, and equipment flows.

"Since these processes are linked to the overall control and assurance of asepsis, the occurrence of even a single contaminated unit in an APS may be indicative of an underlying issue in any one of these systems and should be viewed as a significant event."

Owing to the complexity and interdependencies of all aspects of aseptic processing and the limited diagnostic capability of the process simulation, a correlation between a specific event and a positive unit is challenging. All positive units must be comprehensively investigated using the principles of quality risk management with a purpose of identifying the root cause(s), implementing CAPAs, and verification of the effectiveness and impact of those CAPAs, as applicable.

In the event that a root cause cannot be established, the expectation is that all reasonable potential causal factors of the failure have been considered and steps have been taken to improve any and all identified issues arising from the investigation, including a comprehensive risk assessment.

NOTE: Based on the limitations of aseptic processing, a comprehensive investigation may conclude that the discovery of a single contaminated unit is not indicative of a failed process.

Recurring positive units in successive process simulations indicate a problem and should be investigated and resolved, even when the acceptance criteria are met for each individual simulation.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 零汙染的本質

Acceptance Criteria（驗收標準）在 APS 中等同於：每次執行，汙染單位數 = 0。

但這並不代表製程是「100% 完美無缺」。PDA PtC-1 明確指出，APS 提供的是「additional, but not absolute, assurance」。換言之，APS 通過只表示在那次模擬情境下製程受控，並不能保證真實生產中每支都無菌。

正確的認知框架是：APS 是「周期性佐證」，而非「絕對保證」。無菌保證（Sterility Assurance）的真正基礎是整個系統的設計與管控——設備滅菌、人員訓練、環境監控、設施設計——而 APS 只是其中一個檢核工具。

比喻說明 — 汙染就像劇場後台的失火警報

想像一場外科手術演練（模擬 APS）：整個流程中只要有任何一個步驟發生汙染（哪怕只是一個培養基瓶陽性），就等同於手術演練中有人在無菌區域沒戴手套。

這不一定代表真正手術會失敗，但一定代表有某個環節出了問題——可能是人員行為、可能是設備設計、可能是環境控制。不追根究柢、不提出 CAPA，就直接重跑一次「希望這次過」，是完全不被接受的做法。

這正是 PtC-1 說的：「沒有調查就直接補做 APS = 不可接受。」

公式與思維 — Poisson 統計視角

Poisson 公式：
P(0 個陽性 | N 單位，每單位汙染率 p)
  = e^(−N × p)

範例：
  N = 3,000 單位，p = 0.001（0.1%汙染率）
  P(0 正) = e^(−3,000 × 0.001) = e^(−3) ≈ 0.05 (5%)

意涵：
  若汙染率高達 0.1%，即使填了 3000 支，
  「全部陰性」的機率只有 5% → 跑出 0 正的
  可能性本就極低。
  因此，若真的能跑出 0 正，代表製程汙染率
  遠低於 0.1%，才是有意義的結果。

FDA 立場：
  傾向以 0 positive = pass 作為絕對標準。
  1 positive = 需調查，通常須重新執行。

EU Annex 1 立場（2022版）：
  與 FDA 相近，但允許深入調查後
  基於科學判斷認定「未必代表製程失敗」；
  不過仍須進行完整 CAPA 並重新確認。

重點提示 — 「1 支陽性」的後果

根據 FDA 2004 年無菌製程指引，1 支陽性 = 重大事件，需要：

  • 全面根本原因調查（含 QRM 工具）
  • 制定並執行 CAPA
  • 視情況重新執行多次 APS 以驗證 CAPA 有效性

EU Annex 1 (2022) 語氣相似，但增加一個重要補充：若根本原因無法確立，仍須對所有可能的成因採取行動，不能以「找不到原因」為由放棄改善。

CDMO 業者注意：若客戶的 APS 出現 1 支陽性，影響遠不止於「重跑一次」，整批商業製造批次的上市時程可能延誤數週到數月。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. APS 驗收標準是「零汙染」，但 PtC-1 又說 1 支陽性「可能不代表製程失敗」——這兩個說法矛盾嗎？請解釋其中邏輯。
  2. 若某次 APS 執行 3,000 支，出現 1 支陽性，根本原因調查顯示是某位操作員的手部動作不規範。請問至少需要哪些 CAPA，以及後續應補做幾次 APS？
  3. 為何「連續多次 APS 都各有 1 支陽性但各自未超標」仍屬嚴重問題？
Topic B: Duration of Process Simulations versus Production — APS 時程長度

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What is the appropriate duration of an APS run? How should APS address multiple shifts and campaign production runs?

Recommendation: The duration of the process simulation should be sufficient to adequately challenge the complete aseptic production process. Process simulation should focus on assessing the highest risk events that would be permitted during routine processing.

Human interventions pose a risk to aseptic operation; therefore, consideration should be given to human variability in performance as well as the level of automation and barrier technology. If multiple personnel and shifts are involved, these should be addressed in the risk evaluation and process simulation design. Batches filled over multiple days without intermediate sterilization (i.e., campaign manufacturing) should be evaluated in the risk assessment and process simulation design.

The duration of the process simulation should be risk-based and designed to simulate the conditions that provide the greater likelihood of uncovering process contamination (i.e., worst-case conditions). Each company must determine appropriate rationale and approaches applicable to their unique operations by means of a documented risk assessment and process simulation design.

  • The duration should be long enough to allow the simulation of the predetermined interventions, take into consideration the filling platform (i.e., closed isolators, RABS, automated, traditional/conventional cleanroom, or manual filling operations), as well as other intrinsic characteristics of the containers and closure systems.
  • The duration of the process simulation should be long enough to fill the required number of units to ensure that the necessary activities and interventions are covered (even if longer than normal production).
  • The risk assessment of the aseptic process should determine the number and frequency of interventions for each media fill, as well as any duration-related conditions or activities that should be included in the media fill. For lyophilization processes, consideration should be given to duration-related process variables, such as transport and handling of units and a representative chamber dwell time.
  • Where there are no risk-based duration-related effects, and/or where longer duration does not add any scientific merit, it should not be necessary for a process simulation to be equal to or be longer than the maximum production duration.
  • Operations that extend over multiple days should also include an assessment of the maintenance of environmental conditions over the extended period of time.
  • Manual aseptic filling or closing processes are highly dependent on the operator's individual performance of the process. Therefore, it is recommended that full-duration media fills be used to qualify these processes.

Rationale: Contamination of an aseptic process is primarily a function of events rather than time. Therefore, the duration of the APS should be sufficient to assess the performance of those activities identified in a risk assessment as having the potential to introduce contamination.

Properly designed automation and barrier technology should reduce the frequency of, or risk associated with human interventions. These factors should be addressed in the risk assessment and process simulation design.

Good process design, including human-factor assessment, adherence to first-air principles, training, operations experience, monitoring, and ergonomics, and the scheduling of breaks and rest periods are better tools for controlling the performance of cleanroom operators, operations, and the potential effects of human fatigue, than the passage of longer-duration media fills.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 事件驅動 vs 時間驅動

這是 Topic B 最關鍵的一句話：「Contamination is primarily a function of events, not time.」

汙染的根本風險來自「干預事件」（interventions）——例如人員進出、設備調整、管路重新連接——而不是單純「跑了多少小時」。因此，APS 的長度不是要「等於或超過最長生產時間」，而是要「涵蓋所有高風險事件」。

重要推論：

  • 高度自動化製程（Isolator）：干預少 → APS 可能比生產短，只要事件都被涵蓋
  • 手動充填製程（Manual Filling）：操作員就是最大風險源 → 必須跑全時長（full-duration）
  • 多班次（Multiple Shifts）：不同操作員有不同行為變異 → 都需要被模擬

比喻說明 — 如果演練比演出短，如何驗證真實表演？

想像一部音樂劇的技術彩排（Technical Rehearsal）：目的是確保舞台效果萬無一失。彩排不一定要跑完全劇，但一定要跑到每個「高風險場景」——煙霧機啟動、演員從高處降落、燈光快速切換。

APS 的邏輯相同：不是比賽誰的 Media Fill 跑最久，而是確保每一個「有可能讓汙染溜進去的場景」都被真實挑戰過。如果你的生產有 campaign 製造（連續多天不中途滅菌），那彩排也要跑多天——因為那個「第三天疲勞的操作員」就是風險。

重點提示 — 冷凍乾燥（Lyophilization）的特殊考量

凍乾製程的 APS 有額外挑戰：需要評估「代表性的凍乾艙停留時間（chamber dwell time）」以及容器在艙外的搬運過程。這意味著凍乾的 APS 不只是充填這一步，還包含：

  • 從充填到推入凍乾艙的搬運
  • 凍乾艙內停留（代表性時間）
  • 出艙後加蓋密封

CDMO 在承接凍乾品項時，APS 設計複雜度顯著高於一般液態充填，Protocol 設計需特別謹慎。

實務應用 — CDMO 的 APS 時程設計決策

當客戶帶著一個新品項來詢問「你們的 Media Fill 需要跑多久？」時，正確答案不是一個固定數字，而是：

  1. 先做風險評估：列出所有生產中的干預事件與頻率
  2. 確認填充平台：Isolator / RABS / 傳統潔淨室 / 手動
  3. 確認是否涉及 campaign 製造、多班次、多操作員
  4. 設計 APS 確保涵蓋所有高風險事件（不一定等於最長生產時間）
  5. 有科學文件支撐時程設計的合理性

這一整套文件就是「Process Simulation Design（製程模擬設計）」，是 CDMO 自行準備的文件，不是監管機構提供的。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 某 CDMO 的液態充填製程使用 Isolator，生產批次通常需要 8 小時。他們的 APS 設計為 4 小時，但涵蓋了所有預定干預項目。這樣可以接受嗎？為什麼？
  2. 若改為傳統潔淨室（Conventional Cleanroom）手動充填，同樣 8 小時生產，APS 設計為 4 小時是否合適？請說明理由。
  3. 什麼是「worst-case conditions」在 APS 時程設計中的實際意義？請舉兩個具體例子。
Topic C: Incubation Temperatures — 培養溫度

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What are suitable incubation temperatures for an APS?

Recommendation: Incubation conditions should be suitable for recovery of all potential microbial contamination. Generally, incubation conditions should be not less than 14 days at a designated temperature range between 20°C and 35°C. Each aseptic processing manufacturer should provide a scientific rationale for the selection of the incubation conditions including temperature.

Literature data or growth promotion tests of environmental isolates may be used to support the selection of temperature range. Growth-promoting tests should be performed to confirm the suitability of the incubation temperatures and conditions. This may involve multiple temperatures. When multiple temperatures are used, the sequence and duration of temperature incubation should be justified.

Rationale: Temperature conditions should be selected based on the knowledge of the characteristics of potential contaminants and process conditions. Most mesophilic environmental contaminants will grow at any temperature within the range of 20–35°C spanning 14 days.

If incubation takes place at two different temperatures within the range of 20–35°C, each temperature should include a minimum of seven days each.

The selection of incubation temperature should be qualified through growth promotion testing performed as part of design of the APS incubation procedure.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 為什麼需要兩個溫度？

潔淨室環境中的微生物汙染物大多屬於「中溫菌（Mesophilic Organisms）」，但其最適生長溫度各有不同：

  • 20–25°C（低溫段）：偏好溫度較低的環境菌，例如某些黴菌（Molds）、酵母菌（Yeasts）及皮膚表面的常見菌株
  • 30–35°C（高溫段）：偏好接近人體體溫的腸道菌、葡萄球菌等，這些是人員污染最常見的來源

若只用單一溫度培養，可能無法偵測到在該溫度生長緩慢的物種，造成假陰性。因此，雙溫培養（至少各 7 天）是目前的業界最佳實踐。

比喻說明 — 用兩種培養基「釣魚」

想像你在一個湖裡釣魚，但不知道湖裡有什麼魚。如果你只帶一種魚餌，可能只釣到某些魚種。如果你帶兩種不同的魚餌（一個適合底棲魚，一個適合表層魚），釣到的魚種就更全面。

雙溫培養的邏輯就是如此：用兩種不同的「溫度環境」，讓各類型的微生物汙染物都有機會生長並被偵測到。

培養條件設計規則

標準雙溫培養設計：
  總培養天數 ≥ 14 天
  溫度範圍：20°C – 35°C

  選項 1（建議方案）：
    第 1 段：20–25°C × 7 天
    第 2 段：30–35°C × 7 天
    （順序可調換，需文件支撐）

  選項 2（單一溫度方案）：
    20–35°C 範圍內的任一溫度 × ≥ 14 天
    需附科學文獻或環境菌株生長促進試驗
    作為科學理由

驗證要求：
  Growth Promotion Test（生長促進試驗）
  必須使用以下試驗菌株確認培養基有效性：
  - Staphylococcus aureus（ATCC 6538）
  - Bacillus subtilis（ATCC 6633）
  - Candida albicans（ATCC 10231）
  等 BP/EP/USP 指定菌株

重點提示 — 培養基選擇與生長促進試驗

培養溫度不是唯一要驗證的，培養基本身的「生長促進能力（Growth Promotion）」也需要在每批 APS 使用的培養基批次上驗證。這是確認：

  • 培養基在儲存、配製、充填過程中沒有失去其促進微生物生長的能力
  • 充填完成後的培養基仍具有足夠的營養成分支持生長

常用培養基：SCDA（Soybean Casein Digest Agar/Broth，大豆酪蛋白消化培養液），俗稱 TSB（Tryptic Soy Broth）。適合大多數好氧環境菌的生長。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 某 CDMO 的環境監控（EM）歷史記錄顯示，分離到的菌株全部都是 30–35°C 最適生長，是否可以改為只用 30–35°C 培養 14 天？需要哪些文件支撐？
  2. 雙溫培養的「順序」（先低後高 vs 先高後低）有差別嗎？若要調換順序，需要做哪些事？
  3. 為什麼 Growth Promotion Test 必須對每一批次培養基進行，而不是在開發階段一次性驗證就夠？
Topic D: Incubation of Nonintegral and Rejected Units — 非完整容器與剔退容器的培養

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: Should nonintegral units and/or units that are otherwise procedurally deemed "rejected" units (during routine operations) be incubated and evaluated as part of the APS study?

Recommendation: As part of the APS design, every effort should be made to ensure that all integral media-filled units are incubated. Procedurally defined nonintegral units, which are detected and discarded as part of the routine operation, should not be incubated (e.g., cracked vials or unsealed containers). Units that are rejected for other reasons (e.g., cosmetic or fill volume), which otherwise would not impact container–closure integrity and therefore sterility assurance, should be incubated and included in the study.

The exclusion of any units from incubation requires justification and documentation. It is important to include higher-risk conditions of the operation (e.g., first-filled units following setup operations or following significant interventions), if their inclusion does not introduce an artificially greater challenge to aseptic control than commercial operation (e.g., units removed by an automated process).

Any exclusion of units should be based on the reproducibility of any exclusion in routine production. If written procedures and batch documentation adequately describe the removal of units not filled or sealed during an intervention, then those units do not need to be incubated. However, in no case should more units be removed, or a larger zone cleared, during a media-fill intervention than would be cleared during a production run.

Rationale: The purpose of the APS is to evaluate those production steps that can have an effect on sterility and microbiological contamination of product. All process steps that may have an effect on sterility of the final product should be included in the simulation.

By design, the APS study should include process conditions that provide the most challenge to the aseptic process and product sterility without introducing an artificially stringent challenge.

The incubation of nonintegral units will not provide any meaningful measure of the aseptic process, since these units do not represent either acceptable production practices or acceptable container-closure integrity. The removal of such nonintegral units is appropriate, as failure to do so may inaccurately represent the sterility control of normal operations.

NOTE: Nonintegral units that are not discovered and removed prior to incubation, remain part of the study and, if found to be contaminated, are investigated as positives.

For the APS, other defects that may routinely be rejected during commercial operations, via inspection processes or otherwise (e.g., cosmetic, particulate, and fill-volume defects), should be incubated and included in the evaluation and overall determination of contamination rate.

If a company does choose to incubate integral units that are normally rejected during interventions, the traceability of those units should be maintained in case those units exhibit post incubation contamination. In that case, an investigation of the contamination must be performed.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 什麼是「Integral（完整的）」？

在 APS 語境中，Integral（完整容器）= 已充填且容器密封完整（filled and sealed, no physical breach of container-closure system）。

分類決策樹：

  • 破裂、未封口的瓶 → Nonintegral → 不需培養（培養結果無意義）
  • 外觀缺陷（顆粒、fill volume 偏差、cosmetic）→ 容器仍封口完整 → Integral → 需培養
  • 干預前後「第一支/最後一支」 → 高風險，原則上需培養（除非自動化排除可重現且有文件）

比喻說明 — 餐廳的破盤 vs 賣相不好的菜

想像餐廳的食安衛生稽查：

  • 破掉的盤子裡的食物 → 廢棄，不需要做食安檢驗（相當於 Nonintegral，培養無意義）
  • 賣相不好但盤子完整的菜 → 仍需檢驗食安是否合格（相當於 cosmetic defect，仍需培養）

APS 要測的是「製程是否能防止汙染進入產品」，破掉的容器本身就已不是密閉系統，培養到的陽性說明不了任何製程問題；但賣相差的容器雖然外觀不好，其密封完整性仍代表真實製程狀態，必須納入評估。

重點提示 — 「人工加難」的紅線

PtC-1 特別提到「artificially stringent challenge（人工加難的挑戰）」是不允許的。

什麼是人工加難？例如：

  • APS 中故意多清掉比生產多 3 倍的容器（擴大干預範圍）
  • 故意讓干預事件發生得更頻繁（超過真實生產頻率）

為什麼不可以？因為 APS 的目的是「模擬真實生產」，如果 APS 做到比真實生產更嚴苛，通過了也沒有代表性；如果做比真實生產更寬鬆，則無法保護患者安全。目標是：最壞情況（worst-case），但不超過真實生產可能的範圍。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. APS 執行中，第 15 支（充填開始後的干預後第一支）因 fill volume 偏低被自動系統剔除。這支容器是否需要培養？判斷邏輯為何？
  2. 若某批 APS 中有 5 支未封口的容器（nonintegral）在培養前被發現並移除，這需要如何記錄？若這 5 支未被發現而進入培養箱，後來 2 支陽性，該怎麼處理？
  3. 「人工加難」（artificially stringent challenge）對 APS 有效性有什麼影響？請從監管角度和品質保證角度分別說明。
Topic E: Aseptic Process Simulation Reconciliation — 核對計算

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What are the reconciliation/accountability requirements for APS?

Recommendation: The target for reconciliation of filled units should be 100%. Lacking 100% accountability is a deviation and must be investigated. The number of units rejected should be documented.

At a minimum, the following information should be documented:

  • Number of units filled
  • Number of units rejected and reasons for each rejection
  • Number of units incubated
  • Number of units inspected after incubation
  • Number of units positive for microbial contamination

100% reconciliation of incubated units is required.

Rationale: Since any positive unit in a process simulation would exceed the acceptance criteria, 100% reconciliation/accountability of all incubated units should be the target.

Reconciliation of total processed units can be challenging based upon the variability and accuracy of counting systems, but efforts should be made to account for all units processed within normal production tolerances.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — Reconciliation（核對）的目的

APS Reconciliation（APS 核對）是確保「每一支充填的培養基容器，我們都知道它在哪裡」的過程。

為什麼 100% 核對如此重要？

因為 APS 的驗收標準是「零陽性」。如果有容器無法追蹤（lost accountability），就無法確認這些容器是否為陽性。若它們是陽性的，就可能讓 APS 錯誤地「通過」——這是對患者安全的威脅。

公式與計算 — APS Reconciliation 計算

核對公式：
  充填總數 = 剔退數 + 培養數
  培養數 = 培養後檢驗數
  培養後檢驗數 = 陰性數 + 陽性數

計算範例：
  充填：3,150 支
  剔退（破損/非完整）：30 支
  剔退（fill volume 偏差，仍需培養）：20 支
  ─────────────────────────────
  應培養數 = 3,150 − 30 = 3,120 支
  （含 fill volume 偏差的 20 支）

  培養後檢驗：3,120 支
  陰性：3,120 支
  陽性：0 支

  核對結果：
  3,150（充填）= 30（不培養）+ 3,120（培養）
  ✔ 100% 核對通過

  若培養後只找到 3,118 支（少 2 支）：
  ✘ 偏差！需調查那 2 支去哪裡了。
  （它們可能是陽性——無法排除，
   因此整個 APS 結果存疑）

重點提示 — 「正常生產容差」的解讀

PtC-1 提到充填總數的核對可以有「normal production tolerances（正常生產容差）」，但培養後的 incubated units 核對則是 100% 無容差。

實際意義：

  • 充填計數器可能有 ±0.X% 的機械誤差 → 對「充填數」有一定寬容度
  • 但進入培養箱的每一支都必須有記錄，出培養箱的每一支也必須有記錄 → 進出數量必須 100% 吻合
  • 任何短少都是偏差，必須調查

實務應用 — CDMO 的核對文件設計

建議 APS 批次記錄（Batch Record）中包含一張「APS Reconciliation 表格」，欄位包含：

  • 充填開始 / 結束時間
  • 充填計數器顯示數（含誤差說明）
  • 各原因剔退數（每筆有理由記錄）
  • 送入培養箱的容器批號 / 數量清單
  • 培養箱位置/貨架號
  • 培養結束取出的容器數量清單
  • 陽性 / 陰性判定數
  • 最終核對計算（以公式形式呈現）

這份文件在 FDA 或 EU Annex 1 查廠時是第一個被要求看的 APS 記錄之一。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 某次 APS 充填 5,000 支，剔退 75 支（含 10 支破損、65 支 cosmetic），培養箱放入 4,990 支，培養後取出 4,988 支（短少 2 支）。請判斷此次 APS 的核對狀態，並說明需要採取哪些行動。
  2. 為什麼「incubated units 的核對」比「filled units 的核對」要求更嚴格？
  3. 若充填計數器的機械誤差已知為 ±0.5%，且充填了 4,000 支，充填計數誤差範圍是多少？這是否影響核對結論？
Topic F: Inverting Units Prior to or During Incubation — 培養前後倒置操作

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: Should APS units be inverted prior to or during some or all of the incubation period?

Recommendation: All filled units should be sufficiently manipulated prior to incubation to assure the contact of all sterile surfaces by the growth media. Such manipulations should be documented.

Rationale: A single inversion of test units is typically sufficient to allow the media to contact any microorganisms present on the upper inner surfaces of the container–closure system. Requiring inverted incubation should not be mandatory.

If a method other than inversion (e.g., agitation or swirling) is used, then that method should be demonstrated to show that all interior product-contact surfaces are exposed to media.

For certain complex containers or configurations, inversion alone may not be sufficient to ensure complete media contact. In these cases, special consideration should be given to selecting a dynamic and/or combination of manipulation methods.

NOTE: The integrity of the container-closure system should be assessed in a separate evaluation.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 為什麼需要倒置？

APS 充填的是液態培養基（Liquid Culture Media，如 SCDA/TSB）。充填並密封後，培養基液體主要在容器底部，而瓶蓋（stopper）的內側、上部玻璃內壁等位置不一定有液體接觸。

問題是：如果充填過程中有微生物汙染落在 stopper 內側或上部容器壁，但培養基從未接觸這個位置，微生物就無法生長，陽性就無法被偵測 → 假陰性（False Negative）。

解決方案：充填後、培養前進行至少一次「180° 倒置（inversion）」，讓培養基接觸容器所有內部表面，確保任何微生物都有機會生長並被偵測。

比喻說明 — 油漆刷每個角落

想像用液體清潔劑清洗一個有複雜內部結構的容器（例如有角落、溝槽的瓶子）：如果清潔劑只流到底部，角落和頂端的汙垢就洗不到。

倒置操作就是「讓清潔劑（培養基）流到每個角落」。對於形狀複雜的容器（如預填充注射器、雙腔袋），單純倒置可能還不夠，需要設計特殊的旋轉或搖動方式來確保全面接觸。

重點提示 — 「倒置培養」不是強制要求

PtC-1 明確說：「Requiring inverted incubation should not be mandatory（倒置培養不應作為強制要求）」。

也就是說，倒置的目的是「確保培養基接觸所有內部表面」，達到這個目的即可。如果其他方式（搖動、旋轉）能達到同等效果，且有文件證明，就可以使用其他方式。

對複雜容器（如：有 luer lock 的預填充注射器、雙倉瓶 dual-chamber vial、lyophilization 半封口狀態的特殊容器），需要特別設計媒體接觸方式並進行驗證。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼「培養基接觸所有內部表面」對 APS 偵測能力如此重要？請解釋其與「假陰性（False Negative）」的關係。
  2. 若某廠的 APS 採用預填充注射器（Pre-filled Syringe），單次倒置是否足夠？應如何設計操作程序並驗證培養基接觸的完整性？
  3. 容器密封完整性測試（Container-Closure Integrity Test, CCIT）與 APS 的倒置操作是否相關？兩者分別在驗證什麼？
Topic G: Aerobic versus Anaerobic — 好氧與厭氧

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: When should anaerobic APS fills be performed?

Recommendation: In rare circumstances, where true anaerobic conditions are achieved in production, an anaerobic media (e.g., fluid thioglycolate) should be considered, for example, where production is entirely in an anaerobic environment or where a confirmed, obligate anaerobe was isolated in a sterility test.

Process simulation units should be processed and incubated under aerobic conditions using a general media such as SCDA. In those instances where inert gas headspace is used in production, that gas should be replaced with sterile air during media fills.

NOTE: Nitrogen overlay processes do not represent anaerobic conditions. If inert gas overlay is used in a process simulation, growth-promotion studies should be employed to ensure that inert-gas overlay does not inhibit aerobic or microaerophilic microbiological growth.

Rationale: The purpose of an APS is to assess the ability of the aseptic production process to prevent the introduction of microorganisms. Since that production occurs in aerobic environments, aerobic processes should be used for media fills.

Any isolated microbial contamination that may be present is more likely to consist of aerobes and microaerophilic microorganisms than true anaerobes. Conducting an anaerobic media fill provides little or no significant scientific information, except possibly under the conditions noted in the Recommendation section.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 為何好氧培養就夠了？

大多數藥廠的無菌充填製程是在有氧環境（Aerobic Environment）中進行的——潔淨室的空氣含有大量氧氣，人員皮膚、設備表面的微生物也主要是好氧菌（Aerobes）或微好氧菌（Microaerophiles）。

真正的厭氧菌（Obligate Anaerobes）在有氧環境中無法存活，因此在典型無菌充填設施中幾乎不會出現。若使用厭氧培養基（如 Fluid Thioglycolate）進行 APS，對多數製程而言提供不了更多科學資訊。

比喻說明 — 用正確的工具做正確的事

想像你的廚房（無菌充填室）主要存在的害蟲是蟑螂（好氧菌）。用蟑螂藥（好氧培養基）就能有效偵測和殺滅蟑螂。

但如果你的廚房並沒有深埋地底的厭氧環境，使用針對土壤厭氧菌（Obligate Anaerobes）的特殊捕蟲器，只是多此一舉，既浪費資源又提供不了實質資訊。

唯一需要用厭氧方法的情況是：你確定廚房裡有厭氧蟲——例如真的有厭氧生產製程，或無菌測試真的分離出專性厭氧菌。

重點提示 — 氮氣覆蓋（Nitrogen Overlay）≠ 厭氧條件

許多注射劑產品使用氮氣覆蓋（Nitrogen Overlay）來保護對氧化敏感的藥品。PtC-1 明確指出：氮氣覆蓋不等於厭氧製程。

關鍵點：

  • 在 APS 中，若生產使用氮氣覆蓋，在媒體充填時應改用無菌空氣（Sterile Air）取代氮氣
  • 若硬要保留氮氣覆蓋進行 APS，需要用 Growth Promotion Study 確認氮氣覆蓋不會抑制好氧菌的生長
  • 理由：SCDA（TSB）需要氧氣才能有效支持好氧菌生長；氮氣會抑制這個過程，造成假陰性

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 某客戶的製程是在氮氣覆蓋下充填（保護氧化敏感的蛋白質藥品）。在設計 APS 時，應如何處理這個氮氣覆蓋的問題？至少提出兩個選項並比較其優缺點。
  2. 若某次無菌試驗（Sterility Test）中分離出疑似厭氧菌，這對 APS 設計有什麼影響？需要採取哪些額外行動？
  3. SCDA（Soybean Casein Digest Agar/Broth）在好氧和微好氧條件下均能生長，為什麼它是 APS 的首選培養基？
Topic H: Aseptic Process Simulation Boundaries — APS 範圍界定

原文內容 Original Text

Problem Statement: What are the boundaries for APS? Can the APS be performed in discrete segments?

Recommendation: The APS begins after the sterilization of materials and components and ends with the closure of the final container.
